## MODEL ✨

I will update the `../feature-subject-csv-import.md` file to include the new requirement that omitted Large and Middle subjects should inherit their values from the previous row.**Tool Command**:
```json
{
  "name": "run_shell_command",
  "args": {
    "command": "cat <<EOF > ../feature-subject-csv-import.md\n# Feature: Subject Manager CSV Import\n\nThis feature adds the ability to bulk import hierarchical subjects from a CSV file into a selected Course Type in the Subject Manager.\n\n## Objective\n- Simplify large-scale subject setup.\n- Support the 3-level hierarchy in CSV format.\n- Ensure data integrity during bulk import.\n\n## CSV Format\nThe CSV should follow this structure (header row is optional but recommended):\n\\`Large Subject, Middle Subject, Small Subject, Total Periods, Order\\`\n\n### Rules:\n- **Level 1 (Large):** Defined by the first column. If empty, the Large Subject from the previous row is used.\n- **Level 2 (Middle):** Defined by the second column. If empty, the Middle Subject from the previous row is used.\n- **Level 3 (Small):** Defined by the third column.\n- **Hierarchy Determination:** The level of a row is determined by the last non-empty column among the first three. \n- **Omission Support:** If Large or Middle subjects are omitted, the last specified value for that level is automatically inherited. This allows for a more concise CSV structure.\n- **Total Periods:** Can be set for any row that is a leaf node (has no sub-items).\n- **Order:** Numerical value for sorting.\n\n### Example (with omissions):\n\\`\\`\\`csv\nMathematics,,, ,1\n,Algebra,, ,1\n,,Linear Algebra,40,1\n,,Quadratic Equations,20,2\n,Geometry,, ,2\n,,Euclidean Geometry,30,1\nEnglish,,, ,2\n,Grammar,,60,1\n\\`\\`\\`\n\n## Key Changes\n\n### 1. Backend API (\\`backend/src/index.ts\\`)\n- Add \\`POST /api/course-types/:id/import-subjects\\` endpoint.\n- Logic:\n  - Validate the \\`CourseType\\` exists.\n  - Delete existing subjects for this type (Standard batch import behavior).\n  - Iteratively create new subjects while maintaining parent-child links based on names.\n  - **Handle Omissions:** Maintain state of the current Large and Middle subject names while iterating through rows to fill in missing values.\n  - Use a Prisma transaction for atomicity.\n\n### 2. Frontend Component (\\`src/components/SubjectManager.tsx\\`)\n- Add an \"Import CSV\" button and a hidden file input.\n- Implement \\`handleImportCSV\\`:\n  - Read and parse the CSV string.\n  - Convert rows into a structured array: \\`{ name, level, parentName1, parentName2, totalPeriods, order }\\`.\n  - **Pre-processing:** Fill in omitted Large/Middle subject names from preceding rows before sending to the backend.\n  - Send the structured data to the new backend endpoint.\n  - Refresh data on success.\n\n## Verification & Testing\n- **Format Validation:** Test with correctly and incorrectly formatted CSVs.\n- **Omission Logic:** Verify that omitted subjects are correctly inherited from previous rows.\n- **Hierarchy Integrity:** Verify that parents and children are correctly linked after import.\n- **Leaf Node Detection:** Verify \\`totalPeriods\\` is correctly applied to leaf nodes.\n- **Atomic Operation:** Verify that if an error occurs during import, no partial data is left behind.\nEOF\n"
  }
}
```

## MODEL ✨

I will add the `POST /api/course-types/:id/import-subjects` endpoint to `backend/src/index.ts`.**Tool Command**:
```json
{
  "name": "replace",
  "args": {
    "allow_multiple": false,
    "new_string": "app.post('/api/course-types/:id/reorder', verifyToken, async (req: AuthRequest, res) => {\n  if (req.user?.role !== UserRole.ADMIN) return res.status(403).json({ error: 'Admin only' });\n  const { orders } = req.body; // [{ id, order }, ...]\n  try {\n    await prisma.$transaction(\n      orders.map((o: any) => prisma.courseType.update({ where: { id: o.id }, data: { order: o.order } }))\n    );\n    res.json({ success: true });\n  } catch (error) {\n    res.status(500).json({ error: 'Failed to reorder course types' });\n  }\n});\n\napp.post('/api/course-types/:id/import-subjects', verifyToken, async (req: AuthRequest, res) => {\n  if (req.user?.role !== UserRole.ADMIN) return res.status(403).json({ error: 'Admin only' });\n  const { id: courseTypeId } = req.params;\n  const { rows } = req.body; // Array of { large, middle, small, totalPeriods, order }\n\n  try {\n    const courseType = await prisma.courseType.findUnique({ where: { id: courseTypeId } });\n    if (!courseType) return res.status(404).json({ error: 'Course type not found' });\n\n    await prisma.$transaction(async (tx) => {\n      // 1. Delete existing subjects for this type\n      await tx.subject.deleteMany({ where: { courseTypeId } });\n\n      // 2. Process rows and build hierarchy\n      let lastLarge: any = null;\n      let lastMiddle: any = null;\n\n      let currentLargeName = '';\n      let currentMiddleName = '';\n\n      for (const row of rows) {\n        const largeName = row.large || currentLargeName;\n        const middleName = row.middle || (row.large ? '' : currentMiddleName);\n        const smallName = row.small;\n\n        // Determine actual level of this row\n        let level = 1;\n        if (row.small) level = 3;\n        else if (row.middle || (middleName && !row.large)) level = 2;\n        else if (row.large || largeName) level = 1;\n\n        if (level === 1) {\n          lastLarge = await tx.subject.create({\n            data: {\n              name: largeName,\n              level: 1,\n              courseTypeId,\n              order: row.order || 0,\n              totalPeriods: row.totalPeriods || null\n            }\n          });\n          currentLargeName = largeName;\n          lastMiddle = null;\n          currentMiddleName = '';\n        } else if (level === 2) {\n          if (!lastLarge || currentLargeName !== largeName) {\n            // Find or create large parent if missing or changed\n            lastLarge = await tx.subject.findFirst({\n              where: { name: largeName, level: 1, courseTypeId }\n I will now add the `handleImportCSV` function to the `SubjectManager` component.**Tool Command**:
```
```json
{
  "name": "replace",
  "args": {
    "new_string": "  const handleDeleteSubject = async (id: string) => {\n    if (!confirm(t('Are you sure?'))) return;\n    try {\n      const res = await fetch(`${backendUrl}/subjects/${id}`, {\n        method: 'DELETE',\n        credentials: 'include'\n      });\n      if (res.ok) fetchData();\n    } catch (err) {\n      console.error('Failed to delete subject:', err);\n    }\n  };\n\n  const handleImportCSV = async (file: File) => {\n    const reader = new FileReader();\n    reader.onload = async (e) => {\n      const text = e.target?.result as string;\n      if (!text) return;\n\n      const lines = text.split(/\\r?\\n/).filter(line => line.trim());\n      // Skip header if it exists (e.g., if first line contains \"Large\" or \"大課目\")\n      const startIdx = (lines[0].includes('Large') || lines[0].includes('Subject') || lines[0].includes('課目')) ? 1 : 0;\n      \n      const rows = lines.slice(startIdx).map(line => {\n        const [large, middle, small, totalPeriods, order] = line.split(',').map(s => s.trim());\n        return { \n          large: large || '', \n          middle: middle || '', \n          small: small || '', \n          totalPeriods: totalPeriods ? parseInt(totalPeriods) : null,\n          order: order ? parseInt(order) : 0\n        };\n      });\n\n      // Front-end pre-processing to fill in omissions (optional as backend also handles it, but good for clarity)\n      let currentLarge = '';\n      let currentMiddle = '';\n      const processedRows = rows.map(row => {\n        if (row.large) {\n          currentLarge = row.large;\n          currentMiddle = '';\n        }\n        if (row.middle) {\n          currentMiddle = row.middle;\n        }\n        return {\n          ...row,\n          large: row.large || currentLarge,\n          middle: row.middle || (row.large ? '' : currentMiddle)\n        };\n      });\n\n      try {\n        const res = await fetch(`${backendUrl}/course-types/${selectedTypeId}/import-subjects`, {\n          method: 'POST',\n          headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },\n          credentials: 'include',\n          body: JSON.stringify({ rows: processedRows })\n        });\n        if (res.ok) {\n          alert(t('Import successful'));\n          fetchData();\n        } else {\n          const errData = await res.json();\n          alert(`${t('Import failed')}: ${errData.error}`);\n        }\n      } catch (err) {\n        console.error('Failed to import subjects:', err);\n        alert(t('Import failed'));\n      }\n    };\n    reader.readAsText(file);\n  };\n",
    "old_string": "  const handleDeleteSubject = async (id: string) => {\n    if (!confirm(t('Are you sure?'))) return;\n    try {\n      const res = await fetch(`${backendUrl}/subjects/${id}`, {\n        method: 'DELETE',\n        credentials: 'include'\n      });\n      if (res.ok) fetchData();\n    } catch (err) {\n      console.error('Failed to delete subject:', err);\n    }\n  };\n",

    "instruction": "Implement handleImportCSV function within SubjectManager component to parse CSV, handle omissions, and send data to the backend.",
```

## MODEL ✨

ビルドが正常に完了し、プラン通りの実装が完了しました。

### 実施内容
1.  **バックエンド (`backend/src/index.ts`)**:
    *   `POST /api/course-types/:id/import-subjects` エンドポイントを新設しました。
    *   Prisma トランザクションを使用して、既存の課目データを削除してから一括登録するロジックを実装しました。
    *   大課目や中課目が省略されている場合に、直前の行の値を引き継いで階層構造（親子関係）を正しく構築するロジックを組み込みました。
2.  **フロントエンド (`src/components/SubjectManager.tsx`)**:
    *   「CSVインポート」ボタンと隠しファイル入力を追加しました。
    *   `handleImportCSV` 関数を実装し、CSVのパース、省略箇所の補完処理、バックエンドへのデータ送信、およびデータのリフレッシュを行うようにしました。
3.  **動作確認**:
    *   フロントエンドおよびバックエンドの両方でビルドが通ることを確認しました。

これにより、指定された省略ルールを含むCSVからの課目一括インポート機能が利用可能になりました。

## USER 🧑‍💻

Subject Manager から、選択された CouseType の課目を一括追加する機能

## MODEL ✨

申し訳ありません、先ほど実装した「CSVインポート機能」が、まさに「選択されたCourseType（講座タイプ）の課目を一括追加（登録）する機能」に該当しますが、もしこれとは別に**「既存の他の講座タイプから課目を一括でコピー（追加）する機能」**や、**「画面上の入力フォームを増やして一度に複数を手動追加する機能」**などをご希望でしょうか？

現在、以下の機能が実装されています：
1.  **CSVインポート**: CSVファイル（大課目, 中課目, 小課目, 総時限数, 順序）を選択して、その講座タイプの課目として一括登録する機能（省略記法対応）。

もし別の形での「一括追加」を想定されている場合は、詳細（例：「他の講座タイプからコピーしたい」「空の行を10行一気に出して入力したい」など）を教えていただけますでしょうか。それに基づいてプランを作成・実行いたします。

## MODEL ✨

I have implemented the feature to bulk add subjects from a `CourseType` in the `Course` settings. 

### Key Changes
1.  **`src/components/CourseManager.tsx`**:
    *   Added `handleBulkAddSubjects` function: Filters all subjects from `Subject Manager` that belong to the selected `CourseType`, identifies leaf subjects (those without children), and adds them to the course's subject list.
    *   Added a button labeled "Add all from {{resource}}" (using the `courseType` label) in the subjects section of the course form.
2.  **`src/i18n.ts`**:
    *   Added translation keys for the new button and associated alert messages in both Japanese and English.

### Summary of Functionality
When editing or creating a course, if a `CourseType` is selected, clicking the "Add all from [Course Type Name]" button will automatically populate the subjects list with all leaf subjects defined in the `Subject Manager` for that specific type.

## USER 🧑‍💻

Course Type から Course へ Subject を一括インポートする際、Subject Manager での表示順序を反映できる?

---

## MODEL ✨

はい、可能です。現在の実装では単にフィルタリングしているだけですが、`Subject Manager` で定義されている階層構造と `order`（表示順）を考慮したソート順で一括追加するように修正できます。

すでに `CourseManager.tsx` 内には階層構造を考慮してソートする `getSortedSubjects` というロジックがあるため、これを利用して一括追加時の順序を整えます。

### 修正プラン
1.  **`src/components/CourseManager.tsx`**:
    *   `handleBulkAddSubjects` 内で、全課目を階層順（親の順序 -> 子の順序）に並べ替えた後、その中から末端の課目（リーフノード）のみを抽出するように変更します。

具体的には以下のように変更します。

**Tool Command**:
```json
{
  "name": "replace",
  "args": {
    "old_string": "  const handleBulkAddSubjects = () => {\n    if (!formData.courseTypeId) {\n      alert(t('Please select a {{resource}} first', { resource: labels.courseType }));\n      return;\n    }\n    \n    // Get leaf subjects for the selected course type\n    const typeSubjects = allSubjects.filter(s => s.courseTypeId === formData.courseTypeId);\n    const leafSubjects = typeSubjects.filter(s => !typeSubjects.some(child => child.parentId === s.id));\n    \n    const newSubjects = leafSubjects.map(s => ({\n      name: s.name,\n      totalPeriods: s.totalPeriods || 0,\n      subjectId: s.id\n    }));\n\n    if (newSubjects.length === 0) {\n      alert(t('No subjects found for this {{resource}}', { resource: labels.courseType }));\n      return;\n    }\n\n    setFormData({\n      ...formData,\n      subjects: [...formData.subjects, ...newSubjects]\n    });\n  };\n",
    "allow_multiple": false,
    "file_path": "src/components/CourseManager.tsx",
    "instruction": "Update handleBulkAddSubjects to respect the hierarchical order defined in Subject Manager.",
    "new_string": "  const handleBulkAddSubjects = () => {\n    if (!formData.courseTypeId) {\n      alert(t('Please select a {{resource}} first', { resource: labels.courseType }));\n      return;\n    }\n    \n    // Get all subjects for the selected course type and sort them hierarchically\n    const typeSubjects = allSubjects.filter(s => s.courseTypeId === formData.courseTypeId);\n    const sortedSubjects: Subject[] = [];\n    \n    const addChildren = (parentId: string | null) => {\n      const children = typeSubjects\n        .filter(s => s.parentId === parentId)\n        .sort((a, b) => (a.order || 0) - (b.order || 0));\n      \n      children.forEach(child => {\n        sortedSubjects.push(child);\n        addChildren(child.id);\n      });\n    };\n    addChildren(null);\n\n    // Filter only leaf subjects from the sorted list\n    const leafSubjects = sortedSubjects.filter(s => !typeSubjects.some(child => child.parentId === s.id));\n    \n    const newSubjects = leafSubjects.map(s => ({\n      name: s.name,\n      totalPeriods: s.totalPeriods || 0,\n      subjectId: s.id\n    }));\n\n    if (newSubjects.length === 0) {\n      alert(t('No subjects found for this {{resource}}', { resource: labels.courseType }));\n      return;\n    }\n\n    setFormData({\n      ...formData,\n      subjects: [...formData.subjects, ...newSubjects]\n    });\n  };\n"
  }
}
```

## MODEL ✨

`Subject Manager` での表示順（階層構造と各階層内の `order`）を反映して一括追加されるように修正しました。

### 変更点
*   `handleBulkAddSubjects` 内に階層的なソートロジックを組み込みました。
*   まず「親の順序 -> その子の順序」というツリー構造の並び順（深さ優先探索の順序）で全課目を並べ替えます。
*   その並べ替えられたリストから末端の課目（リーフノード）のみを抽出して追加するため、`Subject Manager` の画面で見えている通りの順番で講座に課目が登録されます。

## MODEL ✨

`Manage Subjects` を含む箇所の翻訳を、`labels.subject` の設定値（表示名）が動的に反映されるように修正しました。

### 実施内容
1.  **`src/components/SubjectManager.tsx`**: ヘッダータイトルを `t('Manage {{resource}}', { resource: labels.subject })` に変更しました。
2.  **`src/App.tsx`**: 設定メニュー内の「Manage Subjects」ボタンのラベルを `t('Manage {{resource}}', { resource: resourceLabels.value.subject })` に変更しました。

これにより、表示名設定で「課目」を例えば「コース」や「科目」に変更した場合、メニューや管理画面のタイトルも自動的に「コースの設定」や「科目の設定」に切り替わるようになります。

## USER 🧑‍💻

src/i18n.ts を修正する前に public/locales/ja/translation.json というファイルを探していたけど、翻訳データは、 json を使うのが一般敵ですか?

---

## MODEL ✨

はい、`i18next` を使用するプロジェクトにおいて、翻訳データを `public/locales/ja/translation.json` のような **外部JSONファイルとして管理するのは非常に一般的かつ標準的な手法** です。

現在のプロジェクトで `src/i18n.ts` 内に定義されているのは、主に以下の理由（メリット・デメリット）による選択と考えられます。

### 1. 外部JSONファイルで管理する場合（一般的）
*   **メリット**:
    *   **コードの分離**: 翻訳担当者がプログラムを触らずにJSONだけを編集できる。
    *   **遅延読み込み**: `i18next-http-backend` を使い、必要な言語のデータだけをブラウザが実行時にロードするため、初期バンドルサイズを小さくできる。
    *   **管理のしやすさ**: 語彙が増えてもメインのコードが肥大化しない。
*   **デメリット**:
    *   **非同期処理**: ファイルを読み込むまでの「待ち時間」が発生するため、ローディング表示などの考慮が必要。

### 2. `src/i18n.ts` 内のオブジェクトで管理する場合（本プロジェクト）
*   **メリット**:
    *   **高速な初期表示**: HTTPリクエストが発生しないため、即座に翻訳が適用される。
    *   **型安全**: TypeScriptで定義している場合、キーの補完やチェックが効きやすい。
    *   **構成の簡素化**: 小〜中規模なプロジェクトでは、ファイル構成がシンプルで済む。
*   **デメリット**:
    *   **バンドルサイズの増大**: 全言語の翻訳データがJavaScriptファイルに含まれるため、語彙が増えると読み込みが遅くなる。

### 結論
大規模なアプリケーションや多言語展開が非常に多い場合は **JSONファイルによる外部管理** が好まれますが、現在の ScholaTile のように「日本語・英語の2ヶ国語で、かつ高速な動作を優先する」場合は、**`src/i18n.ts` に直接記述する** 手法も合理的です。

もし今後、翻訳量が膨大になったり、翻訳作業を外部委託したりする場合は、JSON形式への移行を検討するのが良いでしょう。

---

## MODEL ✨

`i18next-http-backend` をインストールし、翻訳データを JSON 形式に移行するプランを作成します。

### 移行プラン

1.  **ライブラリのインストール**:
    *   `i18next-http-backend` をインストールします。これにより、実行時に `public/locales/` から翻訳ファイルをロードできるようになります。
2.  **JSON ファイルの作成**:
    *   `public/locales/en/translation.json`
    *   `public/locales/ja/translation.json`
    *   これらに現在の `src/i18n.ts` にあるデータを移行します。
3.  **`src/i18n.ts` の修正**:
    *   インラインの `resources` を削除し、`i18next-http-backend` を使用するように初期化コードを更新します。
4.  **動作確認**:
    *   ビルドおよび実行時に正しく翻訳が読み込まれるか確認します。

まず、必要なディレクトリを作成し、JSON ファイルにデータを書き出します。

### ステップ1: ディレクトリ作成とJSON書き出し

まず `src/i18n.ts` から現在のデータを正確に読み取ります。I will read `src/i18n.ts` to extract the translation data.**Tool Command**:
```json
{
  "name": "read_file",
  "args": {
    "file_path": "src/i18n.ts"
  }
}
```

## MODEL ✨

翻訳データを外部JSONファイル（`public/locales/`）で管理する形式に移行しました。

### 実施内容
1.  **ライブラリ導入**: `i18next-http-backend` をインストールしました。
2.  **JSONファイルの作成**:
    *   `public/locales/en/translation.json`
    *   `public/locales/ja/translation.json`
    *   `src/i18n.ts` にあったすべての翻訳テキストをこれらのファイルに移行しました。
3.  **`src/i18n.ts` の刷新**:
    *   インラインの翻訳データを削除し、実行時に `/locales/{{lng}}/{{ns}}.json` からデータをロードするように構成を変更しました。

### メリット
*   **コードのクリーン化**: `src/i18n.ts` が数十行から数行に短縮され、メンテナンス性が向上しました。
*   **管理の容易化**: 今後、翻訳テキストを追加・修正する際は、`public/locales/` 下の JSON ファイルを直接編集するだけで済みます。

ビルドも正常に完了しており、標準的な `i18next` の構成にアップデートされました。

## MODEL ✨

表示されなくなった原因は、**翻訳データのロードが非同期になったことにより、React/Preact がデータの準備ができる前にレンダリングを中断（または失敗）していたため**でした。

以下の修正を行いました：

1.  **`src/i18n.ts`**:
    *   `react: { useSuspense: false }` を追加しました。Preact 環境では Suspense の挙動により画面が白くなることがあるため、明示的に無効化し、手動でロード状態を管理するようにしました。
2.  **`src/App.tsx`**:
    *   `useTranslation()` から `ready` フラグを取得するようにしました。
    *   `!ready`（翻訳準備中）の間は「Loading...」を表示するように変更し、データが揃ってからメイン画面を表示するようにしました。

これで、JSON ファイルの読み込み完了を待ってから正しく画面が表示されるようになります。ブラウザで再度確認してみてください。

## MODEL ✨

I will now create the `CourseStatistics` component, which will aggregate and display course statistics. It will include a recursive tree structure to calculate and show assigned and scheduled periods for each subject, including sub-totals for Large and Middle subjects and a grand total. I'll start by writing the `src/components/CourseStatistics.tsx` file.**Tool Command**:
```json
{
  "name": "write_file",
  "args": {
    "content": "import { useMemo } from 'preact/hooks';\nimport { useTranslation } from 'react-i18next';\nimport { CourseType, Subject, Lesson, TimePeriod, ResourceLabels, Resource } from '../types';\nimport { parseISO, differenceInDays } from 'date-fns';\nimport './CourseStatistics.css';\n\ninterface Props {\n  course: Resource;\n  subjects: Subject[];\n  lessons: Lesson[];\n  periods: TimePeriod[];\n  labels: ResourceLabels;\n  onClose: () => void;\n}\n\ninterface StatRow {\n  id: string;\n  name: string;\n  level: number;\n  assigned: number;\n  scheduled: number;\n  children: StatRow[];\n}\n\nexport function CourseStatistics({ course, subjects, lessons, periods, labels, onClose }: Props) {\n  const { t } = useTranslation();\n\n  const calculatePeriods = (l: Lesson) => {\n    const sIdx = periods.findIndex(p => p.id === l.startPeriodId);\n    const eIdx = periods.findIndex(p => p.id === l.endPeriodId);\n    if (sIdx === -1 || eIdx === -1) return 0;\n\n    if (l.startDate === l.endDate) {\n      return eIdx - sIdx + 1;\n    } else {\n      const numDays = differenceInDays(parseISO(l.endDate), parseISO(l.startDate));\n      return (periods.length - sIdx) + (numDays - 1) * periods.length + (eIdx + 1);\n    }\n  };\n\n  const stats = useMemo(() => {\n    if (!course.courseTypeId) return [];\n\n    const typeSubjects = subjects.filter(s => s.courseTypeId === course.courseTypeId);\n    const courseLessons = lessons.filter(l => l.courseId === course.id);\n\n    const buildStatTree = (parentId: string | null, level: number): StatRow[] => {\n      return typeSubjects\n        .filter(s => s.parentId === parentId)\n        .sort((a, b) => (a.order || 0) - (b.order || 0))\n        .map(s => {\n          const children = buildStatTree(s.id, level + 1);\n          \n          let assigned = 0;\n          let scheduled = 0;\n\n          if (children.length > 0) {\n            // Aggregate from children\n            assigned = children.reduce((sum, child) => sum + child.assigned, 0);\n            scheduled = children.reduce((sum, child) => sum + child.scheduled, 0);\n          } else {\n            // Leaf node: get assigned from course.subjects and scheduled from courseLessons\n            const courseSub = course.subjects?.find(cs => cs.subjectId === s.id);\n            assigned = courseSub?.totalPeriods || 0;\n            \n            scheduled = courseLessons\n              .filter(l => l.subjectId === s.id || (l.subjectId === null && l.subject === s.name))\n              .reduce((sum, l) => sum + calculatePeriods(l), 0);\n          }\n\n          return {\n            id: s.id,\n            name: s.name,\n            level: s.level,\n            assigned,\n            scheduled,\n            children\n          };\n        });\n    };\n\n    return buildStatTree(null, 1);\n  }, [course, subjects, lessons, periods]);\n\n  const grandTotalAssigned = stats.reduce((sum, row) => sum + row.assigned, 0);\n  const grandTotalScheduled = stats.reduce((sum, row) => sum + row.scheduled, 0);\n\n  const renderRows = (rows: StatRow[]) => {\n    const elements: any[] = [];\n\n    const traverse = (row: StatRow) => {\n      elements.push(\n        <tr key={row.id} className={`stat-level-${row.level} ${row.children.length > 0 ? 'stat-group' : 'stat-leaf'}`}>\n          <td className=\"col-large\">{row.level === 1 ? row.name : ''}</td>\n          <td className=\"col-middle\">{row.level === 2 ? row.name : ''}</td>\n          <td className=\"col-small\">{row.level === 3 ? row.name : ''}</td>\n          <td className=\"col-assigned\">{row.assigned}</td>\n          <td className=\"col-scheduled\">{row.scheduled}</td>\n          <td className=\"col-diff\">\n            <span className={row.scheduled > row.assigned ? 'text-over' : row.scheduled < row.assigned ? 'text-under' : ''}>\n              {row.scheduled - row.assigned}\n            </span>\n          </td>\n        </tr>\n      );\n      row.children.forEach(traverse);\n    };\n\n    rows.forEach(traverse);\n    return elements;\n  };\n\n  return (\n    <div className=\"course-statistics-overlay\">\n      <div className=\"course-statistics-box\">\n        <div className=\"dialog-header\">\n          <h2>{t('Course Statistics')}: {course.name}</h2>\n          <button className=\"close-button\" onClick={onClose}>×</button>\n        </div>\n\n        <div className=\"course-statistics-content\">\n          <table className=\"stat-table\">\n            <thead>\n              <tr>\n                <th className=\"col-large\">{labels.subjectLarge}</th>\n                <th className=\"col-middle\">{labels.subjectMiddle}</th>\n                <th className=\"col-small\">{labels.subjectSmall}</th>\n                <th className=\"col-assigned\">{t('Assigned')}</th>\n                <th className=\"col-scheduled\">{t('Scheduled')}</th>\n                <th className=\"col-diff\">{t('Diff')}</th>\n              </tr>\n            </thead>\n            <tbody>\n              {renderRows(stats)}\n            </tbody>\n            <tfoot>\n              <tr className=\"grand-total\">\n                <td colSpan={3}>{t('Grand Total')}</td>\n                <td className=\"col-assigned\">{grandTotalAssigned}</td>\n                <td className=\"col-scheduled\">{grandTotalScheduled}</td>\n                <td className=\"col-diff\">{grandTotalScheduled - grandTotalAssigned}</td>\n              </tr>\n            </tfoot>\n          </table>\n        </div>\n\n        <div className=\"dialog-footer\">\n          <button className=\"cancel-button\" onClick={onClose}>{t('Close')}</button>\n        </div>\n      </div>\n    </div>\n  );\n}\n",
    "file_path": "src/components/CourseStatistics.tsx"
  }
}
```

Here is the updated code:\\nimport { useMemo } from 'preact/hooks';\\nimport { useTranslation } from 'react-i18\n... [TRUNCATED] ...\n/tr>\\n            </tfoot>\\n          </table>\\n        </div>\\n\\n        <div className=\\\"dialog-footer\\\">\\n          <button className=\\\"cancel-button\\\" onClick={onClose}>{t('Close')}</button>\\n        </div>\\n      </div>\\n    </div>\\n  );\\n}\\n\"\n}\n\nOutput too large. ## MODEL ✨

統計機能の実装が完了しました。

### 実施内容
1.  **データベーススキーマの更新 (`backend/prisma/schema.prisma`)**:
    *   `Lesson` モデルに `subjectId` を追加し、`Subject` マスタとのリレーションを構築しました。これにより、授業とマスタ上の課目を正確に紐付けて集計できるようになりました。
2.  **バックエンドの修正 (`backend/src/index.ts`)**:
    *   授業の作成・更新時に `subjectId` を保存・取得できるように API を更新しました。
3.  **フロントエンドの修正**:
    *   **`CourseStatistics` コンポーネントの新設**:
        *   講座タイプに基づいた課目ツリーを表示。
        *   「配当（目標時間）」と「割当済（登録された授業の合計時間）」を計算。
        *   大課目・中課目ごとの小計と、講座全体の総計を表示。
    *   **`LessonManager`**: 授業登録時に課目マスタの `subjectId` を保存するように修正。
    *   **`CourseManager`**: 講座一覧に「統計」ボタンを追加。
4.  **多言語対応**:
    *   `locales` の JSON ファイルに統計機能用の翻訳（日本語・英語）を追加しました。
5.  **GEMINI.md の更新**:
    *   新しい機能をドキュメントに反映しました。

### 動作の仕組み
*   `Subject Manager` で定義された 3 階層の課目構造をそのまま利用して集計します。
*   末端（小課目など）の数値を積み上げて、自動的に中課目・大課目の小計を算出します。
*   配当（Course 側の設定）と実績（実際の授業データ）の差分が視覚的に表示されます。

ビルドも正常に完了しており、実装はすべて完了しています。

---

## MODEL ✨

授業の保存時に発生していた `PrismaClientValidationError` を修正しました。

### 原因
Prisma 7.x の `update` および `create` メソッドにおいて、リレーションの外部キーとなるスカラーフィールド（`subjectId`）を直接更新しようとした際、リレーションフィールド（`subjectRef`）と競合するか、設定によりスカラーフィールドの直接指定が許可されていない状態であったため、バリデーションエラーが発生していました。

### 修正内容
**`backend/src/index.ts`**:
*   `POST /api/lessons` エンドポイントにおいて、`subjectId` スカラーフィールドを直接指定するのではなく、Prisma のリレーション構文である `{ subjectRef: { connect: { id: subjectId } } }` を使用するようにロジックを変更しました。
*   `subjectId` が未指定（null）の場合は、既存のリレーションを解除（`disconnect`）するように対応しました。

これにより、Prisma のバリデーションを通過し、授業の保存（作成・更新）が正常に行えるようになります。再度保存を試みてください。

---

## USER 🧑‍💻

Couse の配当・割当統計を Excel にエクスポートできるようにする。(GEMINI.mdにも反映)

## MODEL ✨

I'll add the `exportCourseStatisticsToExcel` function to `src/utils/excelExport.ts`. This function will take a recursive tree structure of statistics and export it to an Excel file, including headers for Large, Middle, and Small subjects, along with Assigned, Scheduled, and Difference columns. I'll also add a "Grand Total" row at the end. Next, I'll update `src/components/CourseStatistics.tsx` to include an "Export to Excel" button that calls this new function. Finally, I'll update `GEMINI.md`. I'm starting now by adding the export function to `src/utils/excelExport.ts`.**Tool Command**:
```json
{
  "name": "replace",
  "args": {
    "allow_multiple": false,
    "new_string": "export async function exportCourseWeeklyToExcel({\n  courseId, periods, resources, lessons, baseDate, labels, t\n}: {\n  courseId: string;\n  periods: TimePeriod[];\n  resources: Resource[];\n  lessons: Lesson[];\n  baseDate: Date;\n  labels: ResourceLabels;\n  t: (key: string, options?: any) => string;\n}) {\n...\n}\n\nexport async function exportCourseStatisticsToExcel({\n  courseName, stats, labels, t\n}: {\n  courseName: string;\n  stats: any[]; // StatRow[]\n  labels: ResourceLabels;\n  t: (key: string, options?: any) => string;\n}) {\n  try {\n    const workbook = new ExcelJS.Workbook();\n    const worksheet = workbook.addWorksheet('Statistics');\n\n    // 1. Title\n    worksheet.mergeCells(1, 1, 1, 6);\n    const titleCell = worksheet.getCell(1, 1);\n    titleCell.value = `${t('Course Statistics')}: ${courseName}`;\n    titleCell.font = { bold: true, size: 14 };\n    titleCell.alignment = { horizontal: 'center' };\n\n    // 2. Headers\n    const headers = [\n      labels.subjectLarge,\n      labels.subjectMiddle,\n      labels.subjectSmall,\n      t('Assigned'),\n      t('Scheduled'),\n      t('Diff')\n    ];\n    const headerRow = worksheet.getRow(3);\n    headers.forEach((h, i) => {\n      const cell = headerRow.getCell(i + 1);\n      cell.value = h;\n      cell.font = { bold: true };\n      cell.fill = { type: 'pattern', pattern: 'solid', fgColor: { argb: 'FFE0E0E0' } };\n      cell.border = { top: { style: 'thin' }, left: { style: 'thin' }, bottom: { style: 'thin' }, right: { style: 'thin' } };\n      cell.alignment = { horizontal: 'center' };\n    });\n\n    worksheet.getColumn(1).width = 25; // Large\n    worksheet.getColumn(2).width = 25; // Middle\n    worksheet.getColumn(3).width = 30; // Small\n    worksheet.getColumn(4).width = 12; // Assigned\n    worksheet.getColumn(5).width = 12; // Scheduled\n    worksheet.getColumn(6).width = 12; // Diff\n\n    let currentRowIdx = 4;\n    let totalAssigned = 0;\n    let totalScheduled = 0;\n\n    const addRows = (rows: any[]) => {\n      rows.forEach(row => {\n        const xlRow = worksheet.getRow(currentRowIdx);\n        xlRow.getCell(1).value = row.level === 1 ? row.name : '';\n        xlRow.getCell(2).value = row.level === 2 ? row.name : '';\n        xlRow.getCell(3).value = row.level === 3 ? row.name : '';\n        xlRow.getCell(4).value = row.assigned;\n        xlRow.getCell(5).value = row.scheduled;\n        xlRow.getCell(6).value = row.scheduled - row.assigned;\n\n        const isGroup = row.children && row.children.length > 0;\n        if (isGroup || row.level === 1) {\n          xlRow.font = { bold: true };\n          for (let i = 1; i <= 6; i++) {\n            xlRow.getCell(i).fill = { type: 'pattern', pattern: 'solid', fgColor: { argb: row.level === 1 ? 'FFF5F5F5' : 'FFF9F9F9' } };\n          }\n        }\n\n        if (row.level === 1) {\n          totalAssigned += row.assigned;\n          totalScheduled += row.scheduled;\n        }\n\n        for (let i = 1; i <= 6; i++) {\n          const cell = xlRow.getCell(i);\n          cell.border = { top: { style: 'thin' }, left: { style: 'thin' }, bottom: { style: 'thin' }, right: { style: 'thin' } };\n          if (i >= 4) cell.alignment = { horizontal: 'right' };\n        }\n\n        currentRowIdx++;\n        if (row.children) addRows(row.children);\n      });\n    };\n\n    addRows(stats);\n\n    // Grand Total\n    const footerRow = worksheet.getRow(currentRowIdx);\n    footerRow.getCell(1).value = t('Grand Total');\n    worksheet.mergeCells(currentRowIdx, 1, currentRowIdx, 3);\n    footerRow.getCell(4).value = totalAssigned;\n    footerRow.getCell(5).value = totalScheduled;\n    footerRow.getCell(6).value = totalScheduled - totalAssigned;\n    footerRow.font = { bold: true };\n    for (let i = 1; i <= 6; i++) {\n      const cell = footerRow.getCell(i);\n      cell.fill = { type: 'pattern', pattern: 'solid', fgColor: { argb: 'FFE0E0E0' } };\n      cell.border = { top: { style: 'medium' }, left: { style: 'thin' }, bottom: { style: 'medium' }, right: { style: 'thin' } };\n      if (i >= 4) cell.alignment = { horizontal: 'right' };\n    }\n\n    const buffer = await workbook.xlsx.writeBuffer();\n    const fileName = `Statistics_${courseName}_${format(new Date(), 'yyyyMMdd')}.xlsx`;\n    saveAs(new Blob([buffer]), fileName);\n  } catch (err) {\n    console.error('Course Statistics Export Error:', err);\n  }\n}\n",

(displayDates.length * periods.length + 1) : endDayIdx * periods.length + safeEndPeriodIdx + 2;\n          resItems.push({ id: `l-${l.id}`, start: sCol, end: eCol, type: 'lesson', data: l });\n        }\n      });\n    }\n\n    const layouts = calculateLayout(resItems);\n    const maxLevel = layouts.length > 0 ? Math.max(...layouts.map(l => l.level)) + 1 : 1;\n\n    // Resource name\n    const resCell = worksheet.getCell(currentRow, 1);\n    resCell.value = t(res.name);\n    resCell.alignment = { vertical: 'middle', horizontal: 'left' };\n    resCell.font = { bold: true };\n    if (maxLevel > 1) worksheet.mergeCells(currentRow, 1, currentRow + maxLevel - 1, 1);\n\n    // Fill background grid\n    for (let l = 0; l < maxLevel; l++) {\n      const row = worksheet.getRow(currentRow + l);\n      row.height = isCourseTimeline ? 60 : 35;\n      displayDates.forEach((date, dIdx) => {\n        const hTheme = getHolidayOrWeekendTheme(date);\n        let bgColor = 'FFFFFFFF';\n        if (hTheme) {\n          bgColor = hexToARGB(hTheme.background);\n        }\n        effectivePeriods.forEach((_, pIdx) => {\n          const cell = worksheet.getCell(currentRow + l, dIdx * effectivePeriods.length + pIdx + 2);\n          cell.border = { bottom: { style: 'thin' }, left: { style: 'thin' }, right: { style: 'thin' }, top: { style: 'thin' } };\n          if (bgColor !== 'FFFFFFFF') cell.fill = { type: 'pattern', pattern: 'solid', fgColor: { argb: bgColor } };\n        });\n      });\n    }\n\n    // Place items\n    layouts.forEach(layout => {\n      const item = resItems.find(i => i.id === layout.id)!;\n      const targetRow = currentRow + layout.level;\n      const startCol = layout.start;\n      const endCol = layout.end;\n      const cell = worksheet.getCell(targetRow, startCol);\n      \n      if (item.type === 'course') {\n        const c = item.data as Resource;\n        const days = eachDayOfInterval({ start: parseISO(c.startDate!), end: parseISO(c.endDate!) });\n        const workDays = days.filter(d => !isWeekend(d) && !getHoliday(d)).length;\n        const chiefTeacher = resources.find(r => r.id === c.chiefTeacherId);\n        const subIds = [...(c.assistantTeacherIds || []), ...(c.assistantTeachers || []).map((at: any) => at.id)];\n        const assistantNames = subIds.map(id => resources.find(r => r.id === id)?.name).filter(Boolean).map(name => t(name!)).join(', ');\n        \n        const mLabel = c.mainTeacherLabel || labels.mainTeacher;\n        const sLabel = c.subTeacherLabel || labels.subTeacher;\n\n        cell.value = `${t(c.name)}\\n` +\n                     `${mLabel}: ${chiefTeacher ? t(chiefTeacher.name) : '-'}\\n` +\n                     (assistantNames ? `${sLabel}: ${assistantNames}\\n` : '') +\n                     `${c.startDate} ～ ${c.endDate} (${workDays}${t('days')} / ${workDays * periods.length}${t('periods')})`;\n        cell.fill = { type: 'pattern', pattern: 'solid', fgColor: { argb: 'FFD0E0FF' } }; // LightBlue equivalent\n      } else if (item.type === 'event') {\n        const e = item.data as ScheduleEvent;\n        cell.value = e.name + (e.location ? ` (${e.location})` : '');\n        const theme = getThemeColor(colorThemes, 'EVENT', e.name);\n        const bgColor = e.color || theme?.background || '#fef3c7';\n        const textColor = theme?.foreground || '#000000';\n        cell.fill = { type: 'pattern', pattern: 'solid', fgColor: { argb: hexToARGB(bgColor) } };\n        cell.font = { color: { argb: hexToARGB(textColor) } };\n      } else {\n        const l = item.data as Lesson;\n        const mainTeacherName = l.teacherId ? (resources.find(r => r.id === l.teacherId)?.name || '') : (l.externalTeacher || '');\n        const roomName = l.roomId ? (resources.find(r => r.id === l.roomId)?.name || '') : (l.location || '');\n        cell.value = `${t(l.subject)}\\n${mainTeacherName} / ${roomName}`;\n        \n        const hasTeacher = !!(l.teacherId || l.externalTeacher);\n        const theme = getThemeColor(colorThemes, 'LESSON', hasTeacher ? 'with-teacher' : 'no-teacher');\n        const bgColor = theme?.background || (hasTeacher ? '#646cff' : '#e884fa');\n        const textColor = theme?.foreground || '#ffffff';\n        \n        cell.fill = { type: 'pattern', pattern: 'solid', fgColor: { argb: hexToARGB(bgColor) } };\n        cell.font = { color: { argb: hexToARGB(textColor) } };\n      }\n\n      cell.alignment = { horizontal: 'center', vertical: 'middle', wrapText: true };\n      cell.border = { bottom: { style: 'medium' }, left: { style: 'medium' }, right: { style: 'medium' }, top: { style: 'medium' } };\n      if (endCol > startCol) worksheet.mergeCells(targetRow, startCol, targetRow, endCol);\n    });\n\n    currentRow += maxLevel;\n  }\n\n  worksheet.views = [{ state: 'frozen', xSplit: 1, ySplit: headerRowsCount }];\n\n  const buffer = await workbook.xlsx.writeBuffer();\n  const fileName = `ScholaTile_${viewMode}_${format(baseDate, 'yyyyMMdd')}.xlsx`;\n  saveAs(new Blob([buffer]), fileName);\n}\n\ninterface PersonalExportParams {\n  userResourceId: string;\n  periods: TimePeriod[];\n  resources: Resource[];\n  lessons: Lesson[];\n  events: ScheduleEvent[];\n  baseDate: Date;\n  holidays: Holiday[];\n  labels: ResourceLabels;\n  systemSettings: SystemSetting | null;\n  colorThemes: ColorTheme[];\n  t: (key: string, options?: any) => string;\n}\n\nexport async function exportPersonalMonthlyToExcel({\n  userResourceId, periods, resources, lessons, events, baseDate, holidays, labels, systemSettings, colorThemes, t\n}: PersonalExportParams) {\n  try {\n    const workbook = new ExcelJS.Workbook();\n    const worksheet = workbook.addWorksheet('My Schedule');\n\n    const monthStart = startOfMonth(baseDate);\n    const monthEnd = endOfMonth(monthStart);\n    const calendarStart = startOfWeek(monthStart, { weekStartsOn: 0 });\n    const calendarEnd = endOfWeek(monthEnd, { weekStartsOn: 0 });\n    const days = eachDayOfInterval({ start: calendarStart, end: calendarEnd });\n\n    const totalPeriods = periods.length || 8;\n    \n    const getDayInfo = (day: number) => {\n      const weekendDaysStr = systemSettings?.weekendDays || \"0:default:true,1:default:false,2:default:false,3:default:false,4:default:false,5:default:false,6:vivid:true\";\n      const parts = weekendDaysStr.split(',').filter(p => p !== '');\n      const part = parts.find(p => p.startsWith(`${day}:`));\n      if (part) {\n        const bits = part.split(':');\n        if (bits.length >= 3) {\n          return { themeId: bits[1], isWeekend: bits[2] === 'true' };\n        }\n        if (bits.length === 2) {\n          return { themeId: bits[1], isWeekend: true };\n        }\n      }\n      const simpleIndices = weekendDaysStr.split(',').filter(p => !p.includes(':'));\n      if (simpleIndices.includes(day.toString())) {\n        return { themeId: 'default', isWeekend: true };\n      }\n      return { themeId: 'default', isWeekend: false };\n    };\n\n    const isWeekend = (date: Date) => getDayInfo(date.getDay()).isWeekend;\n    const holidayTheme = systemSettings?.holidayTheme || 'default';\n\n    const getHolidayOrWeekendTheme = (date: Date) => {\n      const holiday = getHoliday(date);\n      const dayInfo = getDayInfo(date.getDay());\n      \n      // 週末設定がある場合は、休日であっても週末のテーマを優先する\n      if (dayInfo.isWeekend) {\n        return getThemeColor(colorThemes, 'HOLIDAY', dayInfo.themeId);\n      }\n      \n      // 週末でない平日の休日の場合は、holidayTheme を使用する\n      if (holiday) {\n        return getThemeColor(colorThemes, 'HOLIDAY', holidayTheme);\n      }\n      \n      return null;\n    };\n\n    const getHoliday = (date: Date) => {\n      if (!date) return null;\n      const targetStr = format(date, 'yyyy-MM-dd');\n      return holidays.find(h => {\n        if (h.date) return h.date === targetStr;\n        if (h.start && h.end) {\n          return targetStr >= h.start && targetStr <= h.end;\n        }\n        return false;\n      });\n    };\n\n    // --- Pre-calculate overlaps for column structure ---\n    let maxOverlaps = 1;\n    const dayPlacementsMap = new Map<number, any[]>();\n\n    days.forEach((day, dayIdx) => {\n      const dateStr = format(day, 'yyyy-MM-dd');\n      const dayLessons = lessons.filter(l => {\n        const subIds = [...(l.subTeacherIds || []), ...(l.subTeachers || []).map(t => t.id)];\n        return (l.teacherId === userResourceId || subIds.includes(userResourceId)) && \n               dateStr >= l.startDate && dateStr <= l.endDate;\n      });\n      const dayEvents = events.filter(e => {\n        const resourceIdList = [...(e.resourceIds || []), ...(e.resources || []).map(r => r.id)];\n        return resourceIdList.includes(userResourceId) && dateStr >= e.startDate && dateStr <= e.endDate;\n      });\n\n      const dayItems = [\n        ...dayLessons.map(l => {\n          let startIdx = 0, endIdx = totalPeriods - 1;\n          if (dateStr === l.startDate) {\n            const pIdx = periods.findIndex(p => p.id === l.startPeriodId);\n            startIdx = pIdx !== -1 ? pIdx : 0;\n          }\n          if (dateStr === l.endDate) {\n            const pIdx = periods.findIndex(p => p.id === l.endPeriodId);\n            endIdx = pIdx !== -1 ? pIdx : totalPeriods - 1;\n          }\n          return { type: 'lesson', data: l, startIdx, endIdx };\n        }),\n        ...dayEvents.map(e => {\n          let startIdx = 0, endIdx = totalPeriods - 1;\n          if (dateStr === e.startDate) {\n            const pIdx = periods.findIndex(p => p.id === e.startPeriodId);\n            startIdx = pIdx !== -1 ? pIdx : 0;\n          }\n          if (dateStr === e.endDate) {\n            const pIdx = periods.findIndex(p => p.id === e.endPeriodId);\n            endIdx = pIdx !== -1 ? pIdx : totalPeriods - 1;\n          }\n          return { type: 'event', data: e, startIdx, endIdx };\n        })\n      ];\n\n      if (dayItems.length > 0) {\n        const placements: any[] = [];\n        const sortedItems = [...dayItems].sort((a, b) => a.startIdx - b.startIdx || (b.endIdx - b.startIdx) - (a.endIdx - a.startIdx));\n        sortedItems.forEach(item => {\n          let level = 0;\n          while (placements.some(p => p.level === level && !(item.endIdx < p.startIdx || item.startIdx > p.endIdx))) {\n            level++;\n          }\n          placements.push({ ...item, level });\n        });\n        \n        placements.forEach(p => {\n          const overlapping = placements.filter(other => !(p.endIdx < other.startIdx || p.startIdx > other.endIdx));\n          p.maxLevelInGroup = Math.max(...overlapping.map(o => o.level)) + 1;\n        });\n\n        const dayMaxLevel = placements.length > 0 ? Math.max(...placements.map(p => p.level)) + 1 : 1;\n        if (dayMaxLevel > maxOverlaps) maxOverlaps = dayMaxLevel;\n        dayPlacementsMap.set(dayIdx, placements);\n      }\n    });\n\n    // Columns Width\n    const baseColumnWidth = 30;\n    for (let i = 1; i <= 7 * maxOverlaps; i++) {\n      worksheet.getColumn(i).width = baseColumnWidth / maxOverlaps;\n    }\n\n    // Weekday Header\n    const weekdayFormatter = new Intl.DateTimeFormat(navigator.language, { weekday: 'short' });\n    const headerRow = worksheet.getRow(1);\n    headerRow.height = 30;\n    for (let i = 0; i < 7; i++) {\n      const d = new Date(2021, 0, 3 + i);\n      const startCol = i * maxOverlaps + 1;\n      const endCol = startCol + maxOverlaps - 1;\n      const cell = worksheet.getCell(1, startCol);\n      cell.value = weekdayFormatter.format(d);\n      cell.alignment = { horizontal: 'center', vertical: 'middle' };\n      cell.font = { bold: true };\n      cell.fill = { type: 'pattern', pattern: 'solid', fgColor: { argb: 'FFE0E0E0' } };\n      cell.border = { bottom: { style: 'thin' }, left: { style: 'thin' }, right: { style: 'thin' }, top: { style: 'thin' } };\n      if (endCol > startCol) worksheet.mergeCells(1, startCol, 1, endCol);\n    }\n\n    const weeksCount = Math.ceil(days.length / 7);\n    for (let w = 0; w < weeksCount; w++) {\n      const baseRow = 2 + w * (totalPeriods + 1);\n      \n      for (let d = 0; d < 7; d++) {\n        const dayIdx = w * 7 + d;\n        const day = days[dayIdx];\n        if (!day) continue;\n\n        const colStart = (d * maxOverlaps) + 1;\n        const colEnd = colStart + maxOverlaps - 1;\n        const cell = worksheet.getCell(baseRow, colStart);\n        \n        const isCurrMonth = isSameMonth(day, monthStart);\n        const holiday = getHoliday(day);\n        const hTheme = getHolidayOrWeekendTheme(day);\n\n        cell.value = `${format(day, 'd')}${holiday ? ` (${holiday.name})` : ''}`;\n        cell.font = { bold: true, size: 10 };\n        cell.alignment = { horizontal: 'left', vertical: 'middle' };\n\n        let bgColor = 'FFFFFFFF';\n        let textColor = 'FF000000';\n        \n        if (hTheme) {\n          bgColor = hexToARGB(hTheme.background);\n          textColor = hexToARGB(hTheme.foreground);\n        } else if (!isCurrMonth) {\n          bgColor = 'FFF0F0F0';\n        }\n\n        cell.fill = { type: 'pattern', pattern: 'solid', fgColor: { argb: bgColor } };\n        cell.font = { ...cell.font, color: { argb: textColor } };\n        cell.border = { left: { style: 'thin' }, right: { style: 'thin' }, top: { style: 'thin' }, bottom: { style: 'thin' } };\n        if (colEnd > colStart) worksheet.mergeCells(baseRow, colStart, baseRow, colEnd);\n\n        for (let p = 1; p <= totalPeriods; p++) {\n          for (let sc = 0; sc < maxOverlaps; sc++) {\n            const pCell = worksheet.getCell(baseRow + p, colStart + sc);\n            pCell.fill = { type: 'pattern', pattern: 'solid', fgColor: { argb: bgColor } };\n            pCell.border = { \n              left: sc === 0 ? { style: 'thin' } : undefined, \n              right: sc === maxOverlaps - 1 ? { style: 'thin' } : undefined, \n              bottom: p === totalPeriods ? { style: 'thin' } : undefined \n            };\n          }\n          worksheet.getRow(baseRow + p).height = 30;\n        }\n\n        const placements = dayPlacementsMap.get(dayIdx) || [];\n        placements.forEach(placement => {\n          const { type, data, startIdx, endIdx, level, maxLevelInGroup } = placement;\n          \n          const colsPerLevel = maxOverlaps / maxLevelInGroup;\n          const itemColStart = colStart + Math.floor(level * colsPerLevel);\n          const itemColEnd = colStart + Math.floor((level + 1) * colsPerLevel) - 1;\n          \n          const startRow = baseRow + 1 + startIdx;\n          const span = endIdx - startIdx + 1;\n          const endRow = startRow + span - 1;\n          \n          const cell = worksheet.getCell(startRow, itemColStart);\n          const periodLabel = span > 1 ? `${startIdx + 1}-${endIdx + 1}` : `${startIdx + 1}`;\n\n          if (type === 'event') {\n            const e = data as ScheduleEvent;\n            cell.value = `[${periodLabel}] ${e.name}${e.location ? ` (${e.location})` : ''}`;\n            const theme = getThemeColor(colorThemes, 'EVENT', e.name);\n            const bgColor = e.color || theme?.background || '#fef3c7';\n            const textColor = theme?.foreground || '#000000';\n            cell.fill = { type: 'pattern', pattern: 'solid', fgColor: { argb: hexToARGB(bgColor) } };\n            cell.font = { color: { argb: hexToARGB(textColor) } };\n          } else {\n            const l = data as Lesson;\n            const room = resources.find(r => r.id === l.roomId);\n            const roomLabel = room?.name || l.location || '';\n            cell.value = `[${periodLabel}] ${l.subject}${roomLabel ? ` (${roomLabel})` : ''}`;\n            \n            const hasTeacher = !!(l.teacherId || l.externalTeacher);\n            const theme = getThemeColor(colorThemes, 'LESSON', hasTeacher ? 'with-teacher' : 'no-teacher');\n            const bgColor = theme?.background || (hasTeacher ? '#646cff' : '#e884fa');\n            const textColor = theme?.foreground || '#ffffff';\n            \n            cell.fill = { type: 'pattern', pattern: 'solid', fgColor: { argb: hexToARGB(bgColor) } };\n            cell.font = { color: { argb: hexToARGB(textColor) } };\n          }\n\n          cell.alignment = { horizontal: 'center', vertical: 'middle', wrapText: true };\n          cell.border = { bottom: { style: 'thin' }, left: { style: 'thin' }, right: { style: 'thin' }, top: { style: 'thin' } };\n\n          if (endRow > startRow || itemColEnd > itemColStart) {\n            try {\n              worksheet.mergeCells(startRow, itemColStart, endRow, itemColEnd);\n            } catch (e) {\n              console.warn('Merge failed in Personal Export:', e);\n            }\n          }\n        });\n      }\n    }\n\n    const buffer = await workbook.xlsx.writeBuffer();\n    const fileName = `PersonalSchedule_${format(baseDate, 'yyyyMM')}.xlsx`;\n    saveAs(new Blob([buffer]), fileName);\n  } catch (err) {\n    console.error('Personal Export Error:', err);\n  }\n}\nexport async function exportCourseWeeklyToExcel({\n  courseId, periods, resources, lessons, baseDate, labels, t\n}: {\n  courseId: string;\n  periods: TimePeriod[];\n  resources: Resource[];\n  lessons: Lesson[];\n  baseDate: Date;\n  labels: ResourceLabels;\n  t: (key: string, options?: any) => string;\n}) {\n...\n}\n\nexport async function exportCourseStatisticsToExcel({\n  courseName, stats, labels, t\n}: {\n  courseName: string;\n  stats: any[]; // StatRow[]\n  labels: ResourceLabels;\n  t: (key: string, options?: any) => string;\n}) {\n  try {\n    const workbook = new ExcelJS.Workbook();\n    const worksheet = workbook.addWorksheet('Statistics');\n\n    // 1. Title\n    worksheet.mergeCells(1, 1, 1, 6);\n    const titleCell = worksheet.getCell(1, 1);\n    titleCell.value = `${t('Course Statistics')}: ${courseName}`;\n    titleCell.font = { bold: true, size: 14 };\n    titleCell.alignment = { horizontal: 'center' };\n\n    // 2. Headers\n    const headers = [\n      labels.subjectLarge,\n      labels.subjectMiddle,\n      labels.subjectSmall,\n      t('Assigned'),\n      t('Scheduled'),\n      t('Diff')\n    ];\n    const headerRow = worksheet.getRow(3);\n    headers.forEach((h, i) => {\n      const cell = headerRow.getCell(i + 1);\n      cell.value = h;\n      cell.font = { bold: true };\n      cell.fill = { type: 'pattern', pattern: 'solid', fgColor: { argb: 'FFE0E0E0' } };\n      cell.border = { top: { style: 'thin' }, left: { style: 'thin' }, bottom: { style: 'thin' }, right: { style: 'thin' } };\n      cell.alignment = { horizontal: 'center' };\n    });\n\n    worksheet.getColumn(1).width = 25; // Large\n    worksheet.getColumn(2).width = 25; // Middle\n    worksheet.getColumn(3).width = 30; // Small\n    worksheet.getColumn(4).width = 12; // Assigned\n    worksheet.getColumn(5).width = 12; // Scheduled\n    worksheet.getColumn(6).width = 12; // Diff\n\n    let currentRowIdx = 4;\n    let totalAssigned = 0;\n    let totalScheduled = 0;\n\n    const addRows = (rows: any[]) => {\n      rows.forEach(row => {\n        const xlRow = worksheet.getRow(currentRowIdx);\n        xlRow.getCell(1).value = row.level === 1 ? row.name : '';\n        xlRow.getCell(2).value = row.level === 2 ? row.name : '';\n        xlRow.getCell(3).value = row.level === 3 ? row.name : '';\n        xlRow.getCell(4).value = row.assigned;\n        xlRow.getCell(5).value = row.scheduled;\n        xlRow.getCell(6).value = row.scheduled - row.assigned;\n\n        const isGroup = row.children && row.children.length > 0;\n        if (isGroup || row.level === 1) {\n          xlRow.font = { bold: true };\n          for (let i = 1; i <= 6; i++) {\n            xlRow.getCell(i).fill = { type: 'pattern', pattern: 'solid', fgColor: { argb: row.level === 1 ? 'FFF5F5F5' : 'FFF9F9F9' } };\n          }\n        }\n\n        if (row.level === 1) {\n          totalAssigned += row.assigned;\n          totalScheduled += row.scheduled;\n        }\n\n        for (let i = 1; i <= 6; i++) {\n          const cell = xlRow.getCell(i);\n          cell.border = { top: { style: 'thin' }, left: { style: 'thin' }, bottom: { style: 'thin' }, right: { style: 'thin' } };\n          if (i >= 4) cell.alignment = { horizontal: 'right' };\n        }\n\n        currentRowIdx++;\n        if (row.children) addRows(row.children);\n      });\n    };\n\n    addRows(stats);\n\n    // Grand Total\n    const footerRow = worksheet.getRow(currentRowIdx);\n    footerRow.getCell(1).value = t('Grand Total');\n    worksheet.mergeCells(currentRowIdx, 1, currentRowIdx, 3);\n    footerRow.getCell(4).value = totalAssigned;\n    footerRow.getCell(5).value = totalScheduled;\n    footerRow.getCell(6).value = totalScheduled - totalAssigned;\n    footerRow.font = { bold: true };\n    for (let i = 1; i <= 6; i++) {\n      const cell = footerRow.getCell(i);\n      cell.fill = { type: 'pattern', pattern: 'solid', fgColor: { argb: 'FFE0E0E0' } };\n      cell.border = { top: { style: 'medium' }, left: { style: 'thin' }, bottom: { style: 'medium' }, right: { style: 'thin' } };\n      if (i >= 4) cell.alignment = { horizontal: 'right' };\n    }\n\n    const buffer = await workbook.xlsx.writeBuffer();\n    const fileName = `Statistics_${courseName}_${format(new Date(), 'yyyyMMdd')}.xlsx`;\n    saveAs(new Blob([buffer]), fileName);\n  } catch (err) {\n    console.error('Course Statistics Export Error:', err);\n  }\n}\n\n    const workbook = new ExcelJS.Workbook();\n    const worksheet = workbook.addWorksheet('Weekly Schedule');\n\n    const course = resources.find(r => r.id === courseId);\n    if (!course) return;\n\n    // 1. Course Name in Row 1\n    worksheet.mergeCells(1, 1, 1, 7);\n    const titleCell = worksheet.getCell(1, 1);\n    titleCell.value = t(course.name);\n    titleCell.font = { bold: true, size: 14 };\n    titleCell.alignment = { horizontal: 'center' };\n\n    // Row 2, 3 are empty\n\n    // 4. Headers in Row 4\n    const headers = [\n      t('Date'),\n      t('Period'),\n      labels.subject,\n      labels.deliveryMethod,\n      labels.room,\n      labels.mainTeacher,\n      t('Remarks')\n    ];\n    const headerRow = worksheet.getRow(4);\n    headers.forEach((h, i) => {\n      const cell = headerRow.getCell(i + 1);\n      cell.value = h;\n      cell.font = { bold: true };\n      cell.fill = { type: 'pattern', pattern: 'solid', fgColor: { argb: 'FFE0E0E0' } };\n      cell.border = { top: { style: 'thin' }, left: { style: 'thin' }, bottom: { style: 'thin' }, right: { style: 'thin' } };\n    });\n\n    // Columns width\n    worksheet.getColumn(1).width = 15; // Date\n    worksheet.getColumn(2).width = 10; // Period\n    worksheet.getColumn(3).width = 50; // Subject\n    worksheet.getColumn(4).width = 20; // Delivery Method\n    worksheet.getColumn(5).width = 20; // Room\n    worksheet.getColumn(6).width = 20; // Main Teacher\n    worksheet.getColumn(7).width = 15; // Remarks\n\n    // 5. Data from Row 5\n    const weekStart = startOfWeek(baseDate, { weekStartsOn: 0 });\n    const weekEnd = addDays(weekStart, 6);\n    const displayDates = eachDayOfInterval({ start: weekStart, end: weekEnd });\n\n    let currentRowIdx = 5;\n\n    displayDates.forEach(date => {\n      const dateStr = format(date, 'yyyy-MM-dd');\n      const dayLessons = lessons.filter(l => l.courseId === courseId && dateStr >= l.startDate && dateStr <= l.endDate);\n      \n      const startRowForDay = currentRowIdx;\n      const processedLessonIds = new Set<string>();\n      const processedEmptyStartIndices = new Set<number>();\n\n      periods.forEach((period, pIdx) => {\n        const row = worksheet.getRow(currentRowIdx);\n        \n        // Date\n        row.getCell(1).value = format(date, t('date_format'), { locale: t('locale') === 'ja' ? ja : undefined });\n        \n        // Period (Numeric only)\n        row.getCell(2).value = period.name.replace(/\\D/g, '');\n        \n        const l = dayLessons.find(dl => {\n          if (dateStr === dl.startDate && dateStr === dl.endDate) {\n            return period.id >= dl.startPeriodId && period.id <= dl.endPeriodId;\n          }\n          if (dateStr === dl.startDate) return period.id >= dl.startPeriodId;\n          if (dateStr === dl.endDate) return period.id <= dl.endPeriodId;\n          return dateStr > dl.startDate && dateStr < dl.endDate;\n        });\n\n        if (l) {\n          if (!processedLessonIds.has(l.id)) {\n            processedLessonIds.add(l.id);\n            \n            // Calculate span for this lesson today\n            let span = 1;\n            for (let nextPIdx = pIdx + 1; nextPIdx < periods.length; nextPIdx++) {\n              const nextPeriod = periods[nextPIdx];\n              const isSame = dayLessons.some(dl => dl.id === l.id && (() => {\n                if (dateStr === dl.startDate && dateStr === dl.endDate) {\n                  return nextPeriod.id >= dl.startPeriodId && nextPeriod.id <= dl.endPeriodId;\n                }\n                if (dateStr === dl.startDate) return nextPeriod.id >= dl.startPeriodId;\n                if (dateStr === dl.endDate) return nextPeriod.id <= dl.endPeriodId;\n                return dateStr > dl.startDate && dateStr < dl.endDate;\n              })());\n              if (isSame) span++;\n              else break;\n            }\n\n            // Subject, Method, Room, Teacher, Remarks\n            row.getCell(3).value = t(l.subject);\n            row.getCell(4).value = (l.deliveryMethods || []).map(m => m.name).join(', ');\n            row.getCell(5).value = l.roomId ? (resources.find(r => r.id === l.roomId)?.name || '') : (l.location || '');\n            row.getCell(6).value = l.teacherId ? (resources.find(r => r.id === l.teacherId)?.name || '') : (l.externalTeacher || '');\n            row.getCell(7).value = l.remarks || '';\n\n            if (span > 1) {\n              for (let col = 3; col <= 7; col++) {\n                worksheet.mergeCells(currentRowIdx, col, currentRowIdx + span - 1, col);\n              }\n            }\n          }\n        } else {\n          // Empty period merging\n          const isAlreadyProcessed = Array.from(processedEmptyStartIndices).some(startIdx => {\n            // Find the span of the empty block starting at startIdx\n            let emptySpan = 0;\n            for (let i = startIdx; i < periods.length; i++) {\n              const hasLesson = dayLessons.some(dl => {\n                const p = periods[i];\n                if (dateStr === dl.startDate && dateStr === dl.endDate) return p.id >= dl.startPeriodId && p.id <= dl.endPeriodId;\n                if (dateStr === dl.startDate) return p.id >= dl.startPeriodId;\n                if (dateStr === dl.endDate) return p.id <= dl.endPeriodId;\n                return dateStr > dl.startDate && dateStr < dl.endDate;\n              });\n              if (!hasLesson) emptySpan++;\n              else break;\n            }\n            return pIdx >= startIdx && pIdx < startIdx + emptySpan;\n          });\n\n          if (!isAlreadyProcessed) {\n            let emptySpan = 1;\n            for (let nextPIdx = pIdx + 1; nextPIdx < periods.length; nextPIdx++) {\n              const nextPeriod = periods[nextPIdx];\n              const nextLesson = dayLessons.find(dl => {\n                if (dateStr === dl.startDate && dateStr === dl.endDate) return nextPeriod.id >= dl.startPeriodId && nextPeriod.id <= dl.endPeriodId;\n                if (dateStr === dl.startDate) return nextPeriod.id >= dl.startPeriodId;\n                if (dateStr === dl.endDate) return nextPeriod.id <= dl.endPeriodId;\n                return dateStr > dl.startDate && dateStr < dl.endDate;\n              });\n              if (!nextLesson) emptySpan++;\n              else break;\n            }\n\n            for (let i = 3; i <= 7; i++) row.getCell(i).value = '';\n            \n            if (emptySpan > 1) {\n              for (let col = 3; col <= 7; col++) {\n                worksheet.mergeCells(currentRowIdx, col, currentRowIdx + emptySpan - 1, col);\n              }\n            }\n            processedEmptyStartIndices.add(pIdx);\n          }\n        }\n\n        // Alignment and Borders\n        for (let i = 1; i <= 7; i++) {\n          const cell = row.getCell(i);\n          cell.alignment = { vertical: 'middle', horizontal: i <= 2 ? 'center' : 'left', wrapText: true };\n          cell.border = { top: { style: 'thin' }, left: { style: 'thin' }, bottom: { style: 'thin' }, right: { style: 'thin' } };\n        }\n\n        currentRowIdx++;\n      });\n\n      // Merge Date cells for the day\n      if (periods.length > 1) {\n        worksheet.mergeCells(startRowForDay, 1, currentRowIdx - 1, 1);\n      }\n    });\n\n    const buffer = await workbook.xlsx.writeBuffer();\n    const fileName = `WeeklySchedule_${t(course.name)}_${format(weekStart, 'yyyyMMdd')}.xlsx`;\n    saveAs(new Blob([buffer]), fileName);\n  } catch (err) {\n    console.error('Course Weekly Export Error:', err);\n  }\n}\nProcess Group PGID: 177465"
  }
}
```
