exportPersonalMonthlyToExcel({\n  userResourceId, periods, resources, lessons, events, baseDate, holidays, labels, systemSettings, colorThemes, t\n}: PersonalExportParams) {\n  try {\n    const workbook = new ExcelJS.Workbook();\n    const worksheet = workbook.addWorksheet('My Schedule');\n    const monthStart = startOfMonth(baseDate);\n    const monthEnd = endOfMonth(monthStart);\n    const calendarStart = startOfWeek(monthStart, { weekStartsOn: 0 });\n    const calendarEnd = endOfWeek(monthEnd, { weekStartsOn: 0 });\n    const days = eachDayOfInterval({ start: calendarStart, end: calendarEnd });\n    const totalPeriods = periods.length || 8;\n    const getDayInfo = (day: number) => {\n      const weekendDaysStr = systemSettings?.weekendDays || \"0:default:true,1:default:false,2:default:false,3:default:false,4:default:false,5:default:false,6:vivid:true\";\n      const parts = weekendDaysStr.split(',').filter(p => p !== '');\n      const part = parts.find(p => p.startsWith(`${day}:`));\n      if (part) {\n        const bits = part.split(':');\n        if (bits.length >= 3) return { themeId: bits[1], isWeekend: bits[2] === 'true' };\n        if (bits.length === 2) return { themeId: bits[1], isWeekend: true };\n      }\n      const simpleIndices = weekendDaysStr.split(',').filter(p => !p.includes(':'));\n      if (simpleIndices.includes(day.toString())) return { themeId: 'default', isWeekend: true };\n      return { themeId: 'default', isWeekend: false };\n    };\n    const isWeekend = (date: Date) => getDayInfo(date.getDay()).isWeekend;\n    const holidayTheme = systemSettings?.holidayTheme || 'default';\n    const getHolidayOrWeekendTheme = (date: Date) => {\n      const holiday = getHoliday(date);\n      const dayInfo = getDayInfo(date.getDay());\n      if (dayInfo.isWeekend) return getThemeColor(colorThemes, 'HOLIDAY', dayInfo.themeId);\n      if (holiday) return getThemeColor(colorThemes, 'HOLIDAY', holidayTheme);\n      return null;\n    };\n    const getHoliday = (date: Date) => {\n      if (!date) return null;\n      const targetStr = format(date, 'yyyy-MM-dd');\n      return holidays.find(h => {\n        if (h.date) return h.date === targetStr;\n        if (h.start && h.end) return targetStr >= h.start && targetStr <= h.end;\n        return false;\n      });\n    };\n    let maxOverlaps = 1;\n    const dayPlacementsMap = new Map<number, any[]>();\n    days.forEach((day, dayIdx) => {\n      const dateStr = format(day, 'yyyy-MM-dd');\n      const dayLessons = lessons.filter(l => {\n        const subIds = [...(l.subTeacherIds || []), ...(l.subTeachers || []).map(t => t.id)];\n        return (l.teacherId === userResourceId || subIds.includes(userResourceId)) && \n...\n      });\n      const dayEvents = events.filter(e => {\n        const resourceIdList = [...(e.resourceIds || []), ...(e.resources || []).map(r => r.id)];\n        return resourceIdList.includes(userResourceId) && dateStr >= e.startDate && dateStr <= e.endDate;\n      });\n      const dayItems = [\n        ...dayLessons.map(l => {\n          let startIdx = 0, endIdx = totalPeriods - 1;\n          if (dateStr === l.startDate) {\n            const pIdx = periods.findIndex(p => p.id === l.startPeriodId);\n...\n            endIdx = pIdx !== -1 ? pIdx : totalPeriods - 1;\n          }\n          return { type: 'event', data: e, startIdx, endIdx };\n        })\n      ];\n      if (dayItems.length > 0) {\n        const placements: any[] = [];\n        const sortedItems = [...dayItems].sort((a, b) => a.startIdx - b.startIdx || (b.endIdx - b.startIdx) - (a.endIdx - a.startIdx));\n        sortedItems.forEach(item => {\n          let level = 0;\n          while (placements.some(p => p.level === level && !(item.endIdx < p.startIdx || item.startIdx > p.endIdx))) {\n            level++;\n          }\n          placements.push({ ...item, level });\n        });\n        placements.forEach(p => {\n          const overlapping = placements.filter(other => !(p.endIdx < other.startIdx || p.startIdx > other.endIdx));\n          p.maxLevelInGroup = Math.max(...overlapping.map(o => o.level)) + 1;\n        });\n        const dayMaxLevel = placements.length > 0 ? Math.max(...placements.map(p => p.level)) + 1 : 1;\n        if (dayMaxLevel > maxOverlaps) maxOverlaps = dayMaxLevel;\n        dayPlacementsMap.set(dayIdx, placements);\n      }\n    });\n    for (let i = 1; i <= 7 * maxOverlaps; i++) {\n      worksheet.getColumn(i).width = 30 / maxOverlaps;\n    }\n    const weekdayFormatter = new Intl.DateTimeFormat(navigator.language, { weekday: 'short' });\n    const headerRow = worksheet.getRow(1);\n    headerRow.height = 30;\n    for (let i = 0; i < 7; i++) {\n      const d = new Date(2021, 0, 3 + i);\n...\n      cell.font = { bold: true };\n      cell.fill = { type: 'pattern', pattern: 'solid', fgColor: { argb: 'FFE0E0E0' } };\n      cell.border = { bottom: { style: 'thin' }, left: { style: 'thin' }, right: { style: 'thin' }, top: { style: 'thin' } };\n      if (endCol > startCol) worksheet.mergeCells(1, startCol, 1, endCol);\n    }\n    const weeksCount = Math.ceil(days.length / 7);\n    for (let w = 0; w < weeksCount; w++) {\n      const baseRow = 2 + w * (totalPeriods + 1);\n      for (let d = 0; d < 7; d++) {\n        const dayIdx = w * 7 + d;\n        const day = days[dayIdx];\n        if (!day) continue;\n        const colStart = (d * maxOverlaps) + 1;\n        const colEnd = colStart + maxOverlaps - 1;\n        const cell = worksheet.getCell(baseRow, colStart);\n        const isCurrMonth = isSameMonth(day, monthStart);\n        const holiday = getHoliday(day);\n        const hTheme = getHolidayOrWeekendTheme(day);\n        cell.value = `${format(day, 'd')}${holiday ? ` (${holiday.name})` : ''}`;\n        cell.font = { bold: true, size: 10 };\n        cell.alignment = { horizontal: 'left', vertical: 'middle' };\n        let bgColor = 'FFFFFFFF', textColor = 'FF000000';\n        if (hTheme) { bgColor = hexToARGB(hTheme.background); textColor = hexToARGB(hTheme.foreground); } \n        else if (!isCurrMonth) bgColor = 'FFF0F0F0';\n        cell.fill = { type: 'pattern', pattern: 'solid', fgColor: { argb: bgColor } };\n        cell.font = { ...cell.font, color: { argb: textColor } };\n        cell.border = { left: { style: 'thin' }, right: { style: 'thin' }, top: { style: 'thin' }, bottom: { style: 'thin' } };\n        if (colEnd > colStart) worksheet.mergeCells(baseRow, colStart, baseRow, colEnd);\n        for (let p = 1; p <= totalPeriods; p++) {\n          for (let sc = 0; sc < maxOverlaps; sc++) {\n            const pCell = worksheet.getCell(baseRow + p, colStart + sc);\n            pCell.fill = { type: 'pattern', pattern: 'solid', fgColor: { argb: bgColor } };\n            pCell.border = { left: sc === 0 ? { style: 'thin' } : undefined, right: sc === maxOverlaps - 1 ? { style: 'thin' } : undefined, bottom: p === totalPeriods ? { style: 'thin' } : undefined };\n          }\n          worksheet.getRow(baseRow + p).height = 30;\n        }\n        const placements = dayPlacementsMap.get(dayIdx) || [];\n        placements.forEach(placement => {\n          const { type, data, startIdx, endIdx, level, maxLevelInGroup } = placement;\n          const colsPerLevel = maxOverlaps / maxLevelInGroup;\n          const itemColStart = colStart + Math.floor(level * colsPerLevel);\n          const itemColEnd = colStart + Math.floor((level + 1) * colsPerLevel) - 1;\n          const startRow = baseRow + 1 + startIdx, span = endIdx - startIdx + 1, endRow = startRow + span - 1;\n          const cell = worksheet.getCell(startRow, itemColStart);\n          const periodLabel = span > 1 ? `${startIdx + 1}-${endIdx + 1}` : `${startIdx + 1}`;\n          if (type === 'event') {\n            const e = data as ScheduleEvent;\n            cell.value = `[${periodLabel}] ${e.name}${e.location ? ` (${e.location})` : ''}`;\n            const theme = getThemeColor(colorThemes, 'EVENT', e.name);\n            const bgColor = e.color || theme?.background || '#fef3c7', textColor = theme?.foreground || '#000000';\n            cell.fill = { type: 'pattern', pattern: 'solid', fgColor: { argb: hexToARGB(bgColor) } };\n            cell.font = { color: { argb: hexToARGB(textColor) } };\n          } else {\n            const l = data as Lesson;\n            const room = resources.find(r => r.id === l.roomId), roomLabel = room?.name || l.location || '';\n            cell.value = `[${periodLabel}] ${l.subject}${roomLabel ? ` (${roomLabel})` : ''}`;\n            const hasTeacher = !!(l.teacherId || l.externalTeacher);\n            const theme = getThemeColor(colorThemes, 'LESSON', hasTeacher ? 'with-teacher' : 'no-teacher');\n            const bgColor = theme?.background || (hasTeacher ? '#646cff' : '#e884fa'), textColor = theme?.foreground || '#ffffff';\n            cell.fill = { type: 'pattern', pattern: 'solid', fgColor: { argb: hexToARGB(bgColor) } };\n            cell.font = { color: { argb: hexToARGB(textColor) } };\n          }\n          cell.alignment = { horizontal: 'center', vertical: 'middle', wrapText: true };\n          cell.border = { bottom: { style: 'thin' }, left: { style: 'thin' }, right: { style: 'thin' }, top: { style: 'thin' } };\n          try { worksheet.mergeCells(startRow, itemColStart, endRow, itemColEnd); } catch (e) { console.warn('Merge failed in Personal Export:', e); }\n        });\n      }\n    }\n    const buffer = await workbook.xlsx.writeBuffer();\n    saveAs(new Blob([buffer]), `PersonalSchedule_${format(baseDate, 'yyyyMM')}.xlsx`);\n  } catch (err) { console.error('Personal Export Error:', err); }\n}\n\nexport async function exportCourseWeeklyToExcel({\n  courseId, periods, resources, lessons, baseDate, labels, t\n}: {\n  courseId: string;\n  periods: TimePeriod[];\n...\n  lessons: Lesson[];\n  baseDate: Date;\n  labels: ResourceLabels;\n  t: (key: string, options?: any) => string;\n}) {\n  try {\n    const workbook = new ExcelJS.Workbook();\n    const worksheet = workbook.addWorksheet('Weekly Schedule');\n    const course = resources.find(r => r.id === courseId);\n    if (!course) return;\n    worksheet.mergeCells(1, 1, 1, 7);\n    const titleCell = worksheet.getCell(1, 1);\n    titleCell.value = t(course.name);\n    titleCell.font = { bold: true, size: 14 };\n    titleCell.alignment = { horizontal: 'center' };\n    const headers = [t('Date'), t('Period'), labels.subject, labels.deliveryMethod, labels.room, labels.mainTeacher, t('Remarks')];\n    const headerRow = worksheet.getRow(4);\n    headers.forEach((h, i) => {\n      const cell = headerRow.getCell(i + 1);\n      cell.value = h;\n      cell.font = { bold: true };\n      cell.fill = { type: 'pattern', pattern: 'solid', fgColor: { argb: 'FFE0E0E0' } };\n      cell.border = { top: { style: 'thin' }, left: { style: 'thin' }, bottom: { style: 'thin' }, right: { style: 'thin' } };\n    });\n    worksheet.getColumn(1).width = 15; worksheet.getColumn(2).width = 10; worksheet.getColumn(3).width = 50; \n    worksheet.getColumn(4).width = 20; worksheet.getColumn(5).width = 20; worksheet.getColumn(6).width = 20; worksheet.getColumn(7).width = 15;\n    const weekStart = startOfWeek(baseDate, { weekStartsOn: 0 });\n    const weekEnd = addDays(weekStart, 6);\n    const displayDates = eachDayOfInterval({ start: weekStart, end: weekEnd });\n    let currentRowIdx = 5;\n    displayDates.forEach(date => {\n      const dateStr = format(date, 'yyyy-MM-dd');\n      const dayLessons = lessons.filter(l => l.courseId === courseId && dateStr >= l.startDate && dateStr <= l.endDate);\n      const startRowForDay = currentRowIdx;\n      const processedLessonIds = new Set<string>();\n      const processedEmptyStartIndices = new Set<number>();\n      periods.forEach((period, pIdx) => {\n        const row = worksheet.getRow(currentRowIdx);\n        row.getCell(1).value = format(date, t('date_format'), { locale: t('locale') === 'ja' ? ja : undefined });\n        row.getCell(2).value = period.name.replace(/\\D/g, '');\n        const l = dayLessons.find(dl => {\n          if (dateStr === dl.startDate && dateStr === dl.endDate) return period.id >= dl.startPeriodId && period.id <= dl.endPeriodId;\n          if (dateStr === dl.startDate) return period.id >= dl.startPeriodId;\n          if (dateStr === dl.endDate) return period.id <= dl.endPeriodId;\n          return dateStr > dl.startDate && dateStr < dl.endDate;\n        });\n        if (l) {\n          if (!processedLessonIds.has(l.id)) {\n            processedLessonIds.add(l.id);\n            let span = 1;\n            for (let nextPIdx = pIdx + 1; nextPIdx < periods.length; nextPIdx++) {\n              const nextPeriod = periods[nextPIdx];\n              const isSame = dayLessons.some(dl => dl.id === l.id && (() => {\n                if (dateStr === dl.startDate && dateStr === dl.endDate) return nextPeriod.id >= dl.startPeriodId && nextPeriod.id <= dl.endPeriodId;\n                if (dateStr === dl.startDate) return nextPeriod.id >= dl.startPeriodId;\n                if (dateStr === dl.endDate) return nextPeriod.id <= dl.endPeriodId;\n                return dateStr > dl.startDate && dateStr < dl.endDate;\n              })());\n              if (isSame) span++; else break;\n            }\n            row.getCell(3).value = t(l.subject);\n            row.getCell(4).value = (l.deliveryMethods || []).map(m => m.name).join(', ');\n            row.getCell(5).value = l.roomId ? (resources.find(r => r.id === l.roomId)?.name || '') : (l.location || '');\n            row.getCell(6).value = l.teacherId ? (resources.find(r => r.id === l.teacherId)?.name || '') : (l.externalTeacher || '');\n            row.getCell(7).value = l.remarks || '';\n            if (span > 1) for (let col = 3; col <= 7; col++) worksheet.mergeCells(currentRowIdx, col, currentRowIdx + span - 1, col);\n          }\n        } else {\n          const isAlreadyProcessed = Array.from(processedEmptyStartIndices).some(startIdx => {\n            let emptySpan = 0;\n            for (let i = startIdx; i < periods.length; i++) {\n              const hasLesson = dayLessons.some(dl => {\n                const p = periods[i];\n                if (dateStr === dl.startDate && dateStr === dl.endDate) return p.id >= dl.startPeriodId && p.id <= dl.endPeriodId;\n                if (dateStr === dl.startDate) return p.id >= dl.startPeriodId;\n                if (dateStr === dl.endDate) return p.id <= dl.endPeriodId;\n                return dateStr > dl.startDate && dateStr < dl.endDate;\n              });\n              if (!hasLesson) emptySpan++; else break;\n            }\n            return pIdx >= startIdx && pIdx < startIdx + emptySpan;\n          });\n          if (!isAlreadyProcessed) {\n            let emptySpan = 1;\n            for (let nextPIdx = pIdx + 1; nextPIdx < periods.length; nextPIdx++) {\n              const nextPeriod = periods[nextPIdx];\n              const nextLesson = dayLessons.find(dl => {\n                if (dateStr === dl.startDate && dateStr === dl.endDate) return nextPeriod.id >= dl.startPeriodId && nextPeriod.id <= dl.endPeriodId;\n                if (dateStr === dl.startDate) return nextPeriod.id >= dl.startPeriodId;\n                if (dateStr === dl.endDate) return nextPeriod.id <= dl.endPeriodId;\n                return dateStr > dl.startDate && dateStr < dl.endDate;\n              });\n              if (!nextLesson) emptySpan++; else break;\n            }\n            for (let i = 3; i <= 7; i++) row.getCell(i).value = '';\n            if (emptySpan > 1) for (let col = 3; col <= 7; col++) worksheet.mergeCells(currentRowIdx, col, currentRowIdx + emptySpan - 1, col);\n            processedEmptyStartIndices.add(pIdx);\n          }\n        }\n        for (let i = 1; i <= 7; i++) {\n          const cell = row.getCell(i);\n          cell.alignment = { vertical: 'middle', horizontal: i <= 2 ? 'center' : 'left', wrapText: true };\n          cell.border = { top: { style: 'thin' }, left: { style: 'thin' }, bottom: { style: 'thin' }, right: { style: 'thin' } };\n        }\n        currentRowIdx++;\n      });\n      if (periods.length > 1) worksheet.mergeCells(startRowForDay, 1, currentRowIdx - 1, 1);\n    });\n    const buffer = await workbook.xlsx.writeBuffer();\n    saveAs(new Blob([buffer]), `WeeklySchedule_${t(course.name)}_${format(weekStart, 'yyyyMMdd')}.xlsx`);\n  } catch (err) { console.error('Course Weekly Export Error:', err); }\n}\n\nexport async function exportCourseStatisticsToExcel({\n  courseName, stats, labels, t\n}: {\n  courseName: string;\n  stats: any[];\n  labels: ResourceLabels;\n  t: (key: string, options?: any) => string;\n}) {\n  try {\n    const workbook = new ExcelJS.Workbook();\n    const worksheet = workbook.addWorksheet('Statistics');\n    worksheet.mergeCells(1, 1, 1, 6);\n    const titleCell = worksheet.getCell(1, 1);\n    titleCell.value = `${t('Course Statistics')}: ${courseName}`;\n    titleCell.font = { bold: true, size: 14 };\n    titleCell.alignment = { horizontal: 'center' };\n    const headers = [labels.subjectLarge, labels.subjectMiddle, labels.subjectSmall, t('Assigned'), t('Scheduled'), t('Diff')];\n    const headerRow = worksheet.getRow(3);\n    headers.forEach((h, i) => {\n      const cell = headerRow.getCell(i + 1);\n      cell.value = h;\n      cell.font = { bold: true };\n      cell.fill = { type: 'pattern', pattern: 'solid', fgColor: { argb: 'FFE0E0E0' } };\n      cell.border = { top: { style: 'thin' }, left: { style: 'thin' }, bottom: { style: 'thin' }, right: { style: 'thin' } };\n      cell.alignment = { horizontal: 'center' };\n    });\n    worksheet.getColumn(1).width = 25; worksheet.getColumn(2).width = 25; worksheet.getColumn(3).width = 30;\n    worksheet.getColumn(4).width = 12; worksheet.getColumn(5).width = 12; worksheet.getColumn(6).width = 12;\n    let currentRowIdx = 4;\n    let totalAssigned = 0;\n    let totalScheduled = 0;\n    const addRows = (rows: any[]) => {\n      rows.forEach(row => {\n        const xlRow = worksheet.getRow(currentRowIdx);\n        xlRow.getCell(1).value = row.level === 1 ? row.name : '';\n        xlRow.getCell(2).value = row.level === 2 ? row.name : '';\n        xlRow.getCell(3).value = row.level === 3 ? row.name : '';\n        xlRow.getCell(4).value = row.assigned;\n        xlRow.getCell(5).value = row.scheduled;\n        xlRow.getCell(6).value = row.scheduled - row.assigned;\n        const isGroup = row.children && row.children.length > 0;\n        if (isGroup || row.level === 1) {\n          xlRow.font = { bold: true };\n          for (let i = 1; i <= 6; i++) xlRow.getCell(i).fill = { type: 'pattern', pattern: 'solid', fgColor: { argb: row.level === 1 ? 'FFF5F5F5' : 'FFF9F9F9' } };\n        }\n        if (row.level === 1) { totalAssigned += row.assigned; totalScheduled += row.scheduled; }\n        for (let i = 1; i <= 6; i++) {\n          const cell = xlRow.getCell(i);\n          cell.border = { top: { style: 'thin' }, left: { style: 'thin' }, bottom: { style: 'thin' }, right: { style: 'thin' } };\n          if (i >= 4) cell.alignment = { horizontal: 'right' };\n        }\n        currentRowIdx++;\n        if (row.children) addRows(row.children);\n      });\n    };\n    addRows(stats);\n    const footerRow = worksheet.getRow(currentRowIdx);\n    footerRow.getCell(1).value = t('Grand Total');\n    worksheet.mergeCells(currentRowIdx, 1, currentRowIdx, 3);\n    footerRow.getCell(4).value = totalAssigned;\n    footerRow.getCell(5).value = totalScheduled;\n    footerRow.getCell(6).value = totalScheduled - totalAssigned;\n    footerRow.font = { bold: true };\n    for (let i = 1; i <= 6; i++) {\n      const cell = footerRow.getCell(i);\n      cell.fill = { type: 'pattern', pattern: 'solid', fgColor: { argb: 'FFE0E0E0' } };\n      cell.border = { top: { style: 'medium' }, left: { style: 'thin' }, bottom: { style: 'medium' }, right: { style: 'thin' } };\n      if (i >= 4) cell.alignment = { horizontal: 'right' };\n    }\n    const buffer = await workbook.xlsx.writeBuffer();\n    saveAs(new Blob([buffer]), `Statistics_${courseName}_${format(new Date(), 'yyyyMMdd')}.xlsx`);\n  } catch (err) { console.error('Course Statistics Export Error:', err); }\n}\n"
  }
}
```

---

## MODEL ✨

`src/utils/excelExport.ts` を修正し、構文エラーを解消しました。あわせて `GEMINI.md` も更新済みです。

### 実施内容
1.  **`src/utils/excelExport.ts` の修復**:
    *   前回の `replace` 操作で紛れ込んでいた placeholder (`...`) を排除し、ファイル内容を完全に復元しました。
    *   新機能 `exportCourseStatisticsToExcel` を正しく組み込みました。
2.  **`GEMINI.md` の更新**:
    *   統計情報のエクスポート機能についてドキュメントを追記しました。

これで、`CourseStatistics` 画面から「Excel」ボタンをクリックすることで、配当時間と割当済時間の集計レポート（大・中・小課目の階層構造と小計・総計を含む）を Excel 形式でダウンロードできるようになります。

最後に、修正が正しく反映されているかビルド確認を行います。

**Tool Command**:
```json
{
  "name": "run_shell_command",
  "args": {
    "command": "npm run build && cd backend && npm run build"
  }
}
```

differenceInDays,\n  startOfMonth, endOfMonth, startOfWeek, endOfWeek, eachDayOfInterval, isSameMonth\n} from 'date-fns';\nimport { ja } from 'date-fns/locale';\nimport { TimePeriod, Resource, Lesson, ScheduleEvent, ResourceLabels, SystemSetting, ViewType, ResourceType, Holiday, ColorTheme, ColorCategory } from '../types';\n\ninterface ExportParams {\n  periods: TimePeriod[];\n  resources: Resource[];\n  lessons: Lesson[];\n  events: ScheduleEvent[];\n  viewMode: ResourceType;\n  viewType: ViewType;\n  baseDate: Date;\n  holidays: Holiday[];\n  labels: ResourceLabels;\n  systemSettings: SystemSetting | null;\n  colorThemes: ColorTheme[];\n  t: (key: string, options?: any) => string;\n}\n\nconst hexToARGB = (hex?: string) => {\n  if (!hex) return 'FFFFFFFF';\n  const cleanHex = hex.replace('#', '');\n  if (cleanHex.length === 3) {\n    const r = cleanHex[0] + cleanHex[0];\n    const g = cleanHex[1] + cleanHex[1];\n    const b = cleanHex[2] + cleanHex[2];\n    return `FF${r}${g}${b}`.toUpperCase();\n  }\n  return `FF${cleanHex}`.toUpperCase();\n};\n\nconst getThemeColor = (themes: ColorTheme[], category: ColorCategory, keyOrId: string) => {\n  const theme = themes.find(t => t.category === category && (t.key === keyOrId || t.id === keyOrId));\n  if (theme) return theme;\n  return themes.find(t => t.category === category && t.key === 'default');\n};\n\nexport async function exportTimetableToExcel({\n  periods, resources, lessons, events, viewMode, viewType, baseDate, holidays, labels, systemSettings, colorThemes, t\n}: ExportParams) {\n  const workbook = new ExcelJS.Workbook();\n  const worksheet = workbook.addWorksheet('Timetable');\n\n  const currentViewStart = startOfDay(baseDate);\n  const isCourseTimeline = viewType === 'course_timeline';\n  const effectivePeriods = isCourseTimeline ? [{ id: 'p-all', name: '', startTime: '', endTime: '', order: 0 }] : periods;\n\n  const getDayInfo = (day: number) => {\n    const weekendDaysStr = systemSettings?.weekendDays || \"0:default:true,1:default:false,2:default:false,3:default:false,4:default:false,5:default:false,6:vivid:true\";\n    const parts = weekendDaysStr.split(',').filter((p: string) => p !== '');\n    const part = parts.find((p: string) => p.startsWith(`${day}:`));\n    if (part) {\n      const bits = part.split(':');\n      if (bits.length >= 3) return { themeId: bits[1], isWeekend: bits[2] === 'true' };\n      if (bits.length === 2) return { themeId: bits[1], isWeekend: true };\n    }\n    const simpleIndices = weekendDaysStr.split(',').filter((p: string) => !p.includes(':'));\n    if (simpleIndices.includes(day.toString())) return { themeId: 'default', isWeekend: true };\n    return { themeId: 'default', isWeekend: false };\n  };\n\n  const isWeekend = (date: Date) => getDayInfo(date.getDay()).isWeekend;\n  const holidayTheme = systemSettings?.holidayTheme || 'default';\n\n  const getHolidayOrWeekendTheme = (date: Date) => {\n    const holiday = getHoliday(date);\n    const dayInfo = getDayInfo(date.getDay());\n    if (dayInfo.isWeekend) return getThemeColor(colorThemes, 'HOLIDAY', dayInfo.themeId);\n    if (holiday) return getThemeColor(colorThemes, 'HOLIDAY', holidayTheme);\n    return null;\n  };\n\n  const getHoliday = (date: Date) => {\n    if (!date) return null;\n    const targetStr = format(date, 'yyyy-MM-dd');\n    return holidays.find((h: Holiday) => {\n      if (h.date) return h.date === targetStr;\n      if (h.start && h.end) return targetStr >= h.start && targetStr <= h.end;\n      return false;\n    });\n  };\n\n  const dayCount = (() => {\n    if (viewType === 'day') return 1;\n    if (viewType === 'week') return 7;\n    if (viewType === 'month') return differenceInDays(addMonths(currentViewStart, 1), currentViewStart);\n    if (viewType === '3month' || viewType === '6month') return differenceInDays(addMonths(currentViewStart, viewType === '3month' ? 3 : 6), currentViewStart);\n    if (viewType === 'year' || viewType === 'course_timeline') {\n      const month = systemSettings?.yearViewStartMonth ?? 4;\n      const day = systemSettings?.yearViewStartDay ?? 1;\n      const start = new Date(getYear(baseDate), month - 1, day);\n      const end = new Date(getYear(baseDate) + 1, month - 1, day);\n      return differenceInDays(end, start);\n    }\n    return 1;\n  })();\n\n  const displayDates = Array.from({ length: dayCount }).map((_, i) => addDays(currentViewStart, i));\n  const currentViewEnd = startOfDay(displayDates[displayDates.length - 1]);\n  const filteredResources = resources.filter(r => r.type === viewMode).sort((a, b) => (a.order ?? 0) - (b.order ?? 0));\n\n  worksheet.getColumn(1).width = 25;\n  for (let i = 0; i < displayDates.length * effectivePeriods.length; i++) worksheet.getColumn(i + 2).width = isCourseTimeline ? 4 : 12;\n\n  const locale = navigator.language;\n  const monthFormatter = new Intl.DateTimeFormat(locale, { month: 'short', year: 'numeric' });\n  const dayFormatter = new Intl.DateTimeFormat(locale, { day: 'numeric' });\n  const weekdayFormatter = new Intl.DateTimeFormat(locale, { weekday: 'short' });\n  const dateFormatter = new Intl.DateTimeFormat(locale, { month: 'short', day: 'numeric', weekday: 'short' });\n\n  let headerRowsCount = isCourseTimeline ? 3 : 2;\n\n  if (isCourseTimeline) {\n    const monthRow = worksheet.getRow(1);\n    monthRow.height = 20;\n    let currentMonth: string | null = null;\n    let startCol = 2;\n    let colCount = 0;\n    displayDates.forEach((date, dIdx) => {\n      const monthLabel = monthFormatter.format(date);\n      if (monthLabel !== currentMonth) {\n        if (currentMonth !== null && colCount > 0) {\n          worksheet.mergeCells(1, startCol, 1, startCol + colCount - 1);\n          const cell = worksheet.getCell(1, startCol);\n          cell.value = currentMonth;\n          cell.alignment = { horizontal: 'center', vertical: 'middle' };\n          cell.font = { bold: true };\n          cell.fill = { type: 'pattern', pattern: 'solid', fgColor: { argb: 'FFE0E0E0' } };\n        }\n        currentMonth = monthLabel;\n        startCol = dIdx + 2;\n        colCount = 1;\n      } else colCount++;\n    });\n    if (currentMonth !== null && colCount > 0) {\n      worksheet.mergeCells(1, startCol, 1, startCol + colCount - 1);\n      const cell = worksheet.getCell(1, startCol);\n      cell.value = currentMonth;\n      cell.alignment = { horizontal: 'center', vertical: 'middle' };\n      cell.font = { bold: true };\n      cell.fill = { type: 'pattern', pattern: 'solid', fgColor: { argb: 'FFE0E0E0' } };\n    }\n    const dayRow = worksheet.getRow(2), wkdayRow = worksheet.getRow(3);\n    dayRow.height = 20; wkdayRow.height = 20;\n    displayDates.forEach((date, dIdx) => {\n      const col = dIdx + 2;\n      const dCell = worksheet.getCell(2, col), wCell = worksheet.getCell(3, col);\n      dCell.value = dayFormatter.format(date);\n      wCell.value = weekdayFormatter.format(date);\n      const hTheme = getHolidayOrWeekendTheme(date);\n      [dCell, wCell].forEach(c => {\n        c.alignment = { horizontal: 'center', vertical: 'middle' };\n        c.font = { size: 9 };\n        if (hTheme) { c.fill = { type: 'pattern', pattern: 'solid', fgColor: { argb: hexToARGB(hTheme.background) } }; c.font = { ...c.font, color: { argb: hexToARGB(hTheme.foreground) } }; }\n        c.border = { bottom: { style: 'thin' }, left: { style: 'thin' }, right: { style: 'thin' }, top: { style: 'thin' } };\n      });\n    });\n  } else {\n    const dateRow = worksheet.getRow(1);\n    dateRow.height = 25;\n    displayDates.forEach((date, dIdx) => {\n      const startCol = dIdx * periods.length + 2;\n      const endCol = startCol + periods.length - 1;\n      const cell = worksheet.getCell(1, startCol);\n      cell.value = dateFormatter.format(date);\n      cell.alignment = { horizontal: 'center', vertical: 'middle' };\n      cell.font = { bold: true };\n      const hTheme = getHolidayOrWeekendTheme(date);\n      if (hTheme) { cell.fill = { type: 'pattern', pattern: 'solid', fgColor: { argb: hexToARGB(hTheme.background) } }; cell.font = { ...cell.font, color: { argb: hexToARGB(hTheme.foreground) } }; }\n      if (periods.length > 1) worksheet.mergeCells(1, startCol, 1, endCol);\n    });\n    const periodRow = worksheet.getRow(2);\n    periodRow.height = 20;\n    displayDates.forEach((date, dIdx) => {\n      const hTheme = getHolidayOrWeekendTheme(date);\n      periods.forEach((p, pIdx) => {\n        const cell = worksheet.getCell(2, dIdx * periods.length + pIdx + 2);\n        cell.value = p.name;\n        cell.alignment = { horizontal: 'center', vertical: 'middle' };\n        if (hTheme) { cell.fill = { type: 'pattern', pattern: 'solid', fgColor: { argb: hexToARGB(hTheme.background) } }; cell.font = { color: { argb: hexToARGB(hTheme.foreground) } }; }\n        cell.border = { bottom: { style: 'thin' }, left: { style: 'thin' }, right: { style: 'thin' }, top: { style: 'thin' } };\n      });\n    });\n  }\n\n  const calculateLayout = (items: { id: string, start: number, end: number }[]) => {\n    if (items.length === 0) return [];\n    const placements: { id: string, start: number, end: number, level: number, maxLevelInGroup: number }[] = [];\n    const sortedItems = [...items].sort((a, b) => a.start - b.start || (b.end - b.start) - (a.end - a.start));\n    sortedItems.forEach(item => {\n      let level = 0;\n      while (placements.some(p => p.level === level && !(item.end < p.start || item.start > p.end))) level++;\n      placements.push({ ...item, level, maxLevelInGroup: 0 });\n    });\n    placements.forEach(p => {\n      const overlapping = placements.filter(other => !(p.end < other.start || p.start > other.end));\n      p.maxLevelInGroup = Math.max(...overlapping.map(o => o.level)) + 1;\n    });\n    return placements;\n  };\n\n  let currentRow = headerRowsCount + 1;\n  const row3Items: { id: string, start: number, end: number, type: 'holiday' | 'event', data: any }[] = [];\n  displayDates.forEach((date, dIdx) => {\n    const holiday = getHoliday(date);\n    if (!holiday) return;\n    if (holiday.date && isSameDay(date, startOfDay(parseISO(holiday.date)))) {\n      const startCol = dIdx * effectivePeriods.length + 2;\n      const endCol = dIdx * effectivePeriods.length + effectivePeriods.length + 1;\n      row3Items.push({ id: `holiday-${date.toISOString()}`, start: startCol, end: endCol, type: 'holiday', data: holiday });\n    } else if (holiday.start && holiday.end) {\n      const hStart = startOfDay(parseISO(holiday.start)), hEnd = startOfDay(parseISO(holiday.end));\n      if (isSameDay(date, hStart) || (isSameDay(date, displayDates[0]) && isAfter(date, hStart) && isBefore(date, hEnd))) {\n        const actualStart = isAfter(hStart, displayDates[0]) ? hStart : displayDates[0];\n        const actualEnd = isBefore(hEnd, displayDates[displayDates.length - 1]) ? hEnd : displayDates[displayDates.length - 1];\n        const sIdx = displayDates.findIndex(d => isSameDay(d, actualStart)), eIdx = displayDates.findIndex(d => isSameDay(d, actualEnd));\n        if (sIdx !== -1 && eIdx !== -1 && isSameDay(date, actualStart)) row3Items.push({ id: `holiday-range-${holiday.name}-${date.toISOString()}`, start: sIdx * effectivePeriods.length + 2, end: eIdx * effectivePeriods.length + effectivePeriods.length + 1, type: 'holiday', data: holiday });\n      }\n    }\n  });\n\n  events.forEach(e => {\n    const eStart = startOfDay(parseISO(e.startDate)), eEnd = startOfDay(parseISO(e.endDate));\n    if (isAfter(eStart, currentViewEnd) || isBefore(eEnd, currentViewStart)) return;\n    const resourceIdList = [...(e.resourceIds || []), ...(e.resources || []).map(r => r.id)];\n    if (e.showInEventRow !== false || resourceIdList.length === 0) {\n      const startDayIdx = displayDates.findIndex(d => isSameDay(d, eStart)), endDayIdx = displayDates.findIndex(d => isSameDay(d, eEnd));\n      const sCol = (startDayIdx === -1) ? 2 : startDayIdx * effectivePeriods.length + ((e.startPeriodId && !isCourseTimeline) ? effectivePeriods.findIndex(p => p.id === e.startPeriodId) : 0) + 2;\n      const eCol = (endDayIdx === -1) ? (displayDates.length * effectivePeriods.length + 1) : endDayIdx * effectivePeriods.length + ((e.endPeriodId && !isCourseTimeline) ? effectivePeriods.findIndex(p => p.id === e.endPeriodId) : effectivePeriods.length - 1) + 2;\n      row3Items.push({ id: `event-${e.id}`, start: sCol, end: eCol, type: 'event', data: e });\n    }\n  });\n\n  const row3Layouts = calculateLayout(row3Items);\n  const row3MaxLevel = row3Layouts.length > 0 ? Math.max(...row3Layouts.map(l => l.level)) + 1 : 1;\n\n  const eventLabelCell = worksheet.getCell(currentRow, 1);\n  eventLabelCell.value = labels.event;\n  eventLabelCell.alignment = { vertical: 'middle', horizontal: 'left' };\n  eventLabelCell.font = { bold: true };\n  if (row3MaxLevel > 1) worksheet.mergeCells(currentRow, 1, currentRow + row3MaxLevel - 1, 1);\n\n  for (let l = 0; l < row3MaxLevel; l++) {\n    const row = worksheet.getRow(currentRow + l);\n    row.height = 35;\n    displayDates.forEach((date, dIdx) => {\n      const hTheme = getHolidayOrWeekendTheme(date);\n      let bgColor = hTheme ? hexToARGB(hTheme.background) : 'FFFFFFFF';\n      effectivePeriods.forEach((_, pIdx) => {\n        const cell = worksheet.getCell(currentRow + l, dIdx * effectivePeriods.length + pIdx + 2);\n        cell.border = { bottom: { style: 'thin' }, left: { style: 'thin' }, right: { style: 'thin' }, top: { style: 'thin' } };\n        if (bgColor !== 'FFFFFFFF') cell.fill = { type: 'pattern', pattern: 'solid', fgColor: { argb: bgColor } };\n      });\n    });\n  }\n\n  row3Layouts.forEach(layout => {\n    const item = row3Items.find(i => i.id === layout.id)!;\n    const targetRow = currentRow + layout.level;\n    const cell = worksheet.getCell(targetRow, layout.start);\n    if (item.type === 'holiday') {\n      const h = item.data;\n      cell.value = h.name;\n      const hTheme = getHolidayOrWeekendTheme(h.date ? parseISO(h.date) : (h.start ? parseISO(h.start) : new Date()));\n      if (hTheme) { cell.fill = { type: 'pattern', pattern: 'solid', fgColor: { argb: hexToARGB(hTheme.background) } }; cell.font = { color: { argb: hexToARGB(hTheme.foreground) }, bold: true }; }\n      else { cell.fill = { type: 'pattern', pattern: 'solid', fgColor: { argb: 'FF8B0000' } }; cell.font = { color: { argb: 'FFFFFFFF' }, bold: true }; }\n    } else {\n      const e = item.data as ScheduleEvent;\n      cell.value = e.name + (e.location ? ` (${e.location})` : '');\n      const theme = getThemeColor(colorThemes, 'EVENT', e.name);\n      const bgColor = e.color || theme?.background || '#fef3c7', textColor = theme?.foreground || '#000000';\n      cell.fill = { type: 'pattern', pattern: 'solid', fgColor: { argb: hexToARGB(bgColor) } };\n      cell.font = { color: { argb: hexToARGB(textColor) } };\n    }\n    cell.alignment = { horizontal: 'center', vertical: 'middle', wrapText: true };\n    cell.border = { bottom: { style: 'medium' }, left: { style: 'medium' }, right: { style: 'medium' }, top: { style: 'medium' } };\n    if (item.end > item.start) worksheet.mergeCells(targetRow, item.start, targetRow, item.end);\n  });\n\n  currentRow += row3MaxLevel;\n  for (const res of filteredResources) {\n    const resItems: { id: string, start: number, end: number, type: 'event' | 'lesson' | 'course', data: any }[] = [];\n    if (isCourseTimeline) {\n      const allCourses = resources.filter(r => r.type === 'course' && r.startDate && r.endDate);\n      let relatedCourses = (viewMode === 'course') ? [res] : (viewMode === 'teacher' ? allCourses.filter(c => c.chiefTeacherId === res.id || c.assistantTeacherIds?.includes(res.id) || (c as any).assistantTeachers?.some((at: any) => at.id === res.id)) : (viewMode === 'room' ? allCourses.filter(c => c.mainRoomId === res.id) : []));\n      relatedCourses.forEach(c => {\n        const cStart = startOfDay(parseISO(c.startDate!)), cEnd = startOfDay(parseISO(c.endDate!));\n        if (isAfter(cStart, currentViewEnd) || isBefore(cEnd, currentViewStart)) return;\n        const sIdx = displayDates.findIndex(d => isSameDay(d, cStart)), eIdx = displayDates.findIndex(d => isSameDay(d, cEnd));\n        resItems.push({ id: `c-${c.id}`, start: (sIdx === -1) ? 2 : sIdx + 2, end: (eIdx === -1) ? (displayDates.length + 1) : eIdx + 2, type: 'course', data: c });\n      });\n    } else {\n      events.forEach(e => {\n        const resourceIdList = [...(e.resourceIds || []), ...(e.resources || []).map(r => r.id)];\n        if (resourceIdList.includes(res.id)) {\n          const eStart = startOfDay(parseISO(e.startDate)), eEnd = startOfDay(parseISO(e.endDate));\n          if (isAfter(eStart, currentViewEnd) || isBefore(eEnd, currentViewStart)) return;\n          const startDayIdx = displayDates.findIndex(d => isSameDay(d, eStart)), endDayIdx = displayDates.findIndex(d => isSameDay(d, eEnd));\n          const sCol = (startDayIdx === -1) ? 2 : startDayIdx * periods.length + (e.startPeriodId ? periods.findIndex(p => p.id === e.startPeriodId) : 0) + 2;\n          const eCol = (endDayIdx === -1) ? (displayDates.length * periods.length + 1) : endDayIdx * periods.length + (e.endPeriodId ? periods.findIndex(p => p.id === e.endPeriodId) : periods.length - 1) + 2;\n          resItems.push({ id: `e-${e.id}`, start: sCol, end: eCol, type: 'event', data: e });\n        }\n      });\n      lessons.forEach(l => {\n        const lStart = startOfDay(parseISO(l.startDate)), lEnd = startOfDay(parseISO(l.endDate));\n        if (isAfter(lStart, currentViewEnd) || isBefore(lEnd, currentViewStart)) return;\n        const subIds = [...(l.subTeacherIds || []), ...(l.subTeachers || []).map(t => t.id)];\n        if ((viewMode === 'room' && l.roomId === res.id) || (viewMode === 'teacher' && (l.teacherId === res.id || subIds.includes(res.id))) || (viewMode === 'course' && l.courseId === res.id)) {\n          const startDayIdx = displayDates.findIndex(d => isSameDay(d, lStart)), endDayIdx = displayDates.findIndex(d => isSameDay(d, lEnd));\n          const sCol = (startDayIdx === -1) ? 2 : startDayIdx * periods.length + (l.startPeriodId ? periods.findIndex(p => p.id === l.startPeriodId) : 0) + 2;\n          const eCol = (endDayIdx === -1) ? (displayDates.length * periods.length + 1) : endDayIdx * periods.length + (l.endPeriodId ? periods.findIndex(p => p.id === l.endPeriodId) : periods.length - 1) + 2;\n          resItems.push({ id: `l-${l.id}`, start: sCol, end: eCol, type: 'lesson', data: l });\n        }\n      });\n    }\n    const layouts = calculateLayout(resItems);\n    const maxLevel = layouts.length > 0 ? Math.max(...layouts.map(l => l.level)) + 1 : 1;\n    const resCell = worksheet.getCell(currentRow, 1);\n    resCell.value = t(res.name); resCell.alignment = { vertical: 'middle', horizontal: 'left' }; resCell.font = { bold: true };\n    if (maxLevel > 1) worksheet.mergeCells(currentRow, 1, currentRow + maxLevel - 1, 1);\n    for (let l = 0; l < maxLevel; l++) {\n      const row = worksheet.getRow(currentRow + l);\n      row.height = isCourseTimeline ? 60 : 35;\n      displayDates.forEach((date, dIdx) => {\n        const hTheme = getHolidayOrWeekendTheme(date);\n        let bgColor = hTheme ? hexToARGB(hTheme.background) : 'FFFFFFFF';\n        effectivePeriods.forEach((_, pIdx) => {\n          const cell = worksheet.getCell(currentRow + l, dIdx * effectivePeriods.length + pIdx + 2);\n          cell.border = { bottom: { style: 'thin' }, left: { style: 'thin' }, right: { style: 'thin' }, top: { style: 'thin' } };\n          if (bgColor !== 'FFFFFFFF') cell.fill = { type: 'pattern', pattern: 'solid', fgColor: { argb: bgColor } };\n        });\n      });\n    }\n    layouts.forEach(layout => {\n      const item = resItems.find(i => i.id === layout.id)!;\n      const targetRow = currentRow + layout.level, cell = worksheet.getCell(targetRow, layout.start);\n      if (item.type === 'course') {\n        const c = item.data as Resource;\n        const days = eachDayOfInterval({ start: parseISO(c.startDate!), end: parseISO(c.endDate!) });\n        const workDays = days.filter(d => !isWeekend(d) && !getHoliday(d)).length;\n        const chiefTeacher = resources.find(r => r.id === c.chiefTeacherId);\n        const subIds = [...(c.assistantTeacherIds || []), ...(c.assistantTeachers || []).map((at: any) => at.id)];\n        const assistantNames = subIds.map(id => resources.find(r => r.id === id)?.name).filter(Boolean).map(name => t(name!)).join(', ');\n        const mLabel = c.mainTeacherLabel || labels.mainTeacher, sLabel = c.subTeacherLabel || labels.subTeacher;\n        cell.value = `${t(c.name)}\\n${mLabel}: ${chiefTeacher ? t(chiefTeacher.name) : '-'}\\n${assistantNames ? `${sLabel}: ${assistantNames}\\n` : ''}${c.startDate} ～ ${c.endDate} (${workDays}${t('days')} / ${workDays * periods.length}${t('periods')})`;\n        cell.fill = { type: 'pattern', pattern: 'solid', fgColor: { argb: 'FFD0E0FF' } };\n      } else if (item.type === 'event') {\n        const e = item.data as ScheduleEvent;\n        cell.value = e.name + (e.location ? ` (${e.location})` : '');\n        const theme = getThemeColor(colorThemes, 'EVENT', e.name);\n        const bgColor = e.color || theme?.background || '#fef3c7', textColor = theme?.foreground || '#000000';\n        cell.fill = { type: 'pattern', pattern: 'solid', fgColor: { argb: hexToARGB(bgColor) } };\n        cell.font = { color: { argb: hexToARGB(textColor) } };\n      } else {\n        const l = item.data as Lesson;\n        const mainTeacherName = l.teacherId ? (resources.find(r => r.id === l.teacherId)?.name || '') : (l.externalTeacher || '');\n        const roomName = l.roomId ? (resources.find(r => r.id === l.roomId)?.name || '') : (l.location || '');\n        cell.value = `${t(l.subject)}\\n${mainTeacherName} / ${roomName}`;\n        const hasTeacher = !!(l.teacherId || l.externalTeacher);\n        const theme = getThemeColor(colorThemes, 'LESSON', hasTeacher ? 'with-teacher' : 'no-teacher');\n        const bgColor = theme?.background || (hasTeacher ? '#646cff' : '#e884fa'), textColor = theme?.foreground || '#ffffff';\n        cell.fill = { type: 'pattern', pattern: 'solid', fgColor: { argb: hexToARGB(bgColor) } };\n        cell.font = { color: { argb: hexToARGB(textColor) } };\n      }\n      cell.alignment = { horizontal: 'center', vertical: 'middle', wrapText: true };\n      cell.border = { bottom: { style: 'medium' }, left: { style: 'medium' }, right: { style: 'medium' }, top: { style: 'medium' } };\n      if (item.end > item.start) worksheet.mergeCells(targetRow, item.start, targetRow, item.end);\n    });\n    currentRow += maxLevel;\n  }\n  worksheet.views = [{ state: 'frozen', xSplit: 1, ySplit: headerRowsCount }];\n  const buffer = await workbook.xlsx.writeBuffer();\n  saveAs(new Blob([buffer]), `ScholaTile_${viewMode}_${format(baseDate, 'yyyyMMdd')}.xlsx`);\n}\n\nexport async function exportPersonalMonthlyToExcel({\n  userResourceId, periods, resources, lessons, events, baseDate, holidays, labels, systemSettings, colorThemes, t\n}: PersonalExportParams) {\n  try {\n    const workbook = new ExcelJS.Workbook();\n    const worksheet = workbook.addWorksheet('My Schedule');\n    const monthStart = startOfMonth(baseDate);\n    const monthEnd = endOfMonth(monthStart);\n    const calendarStart = startOfWeek(monthStart, { weekStartsOn: 0 });\n    const calendarEnd = endOfWeek(monthEnd, { weekStartsOn: 0 });\n    const days = eachDayOfInterval({ start: calendarStart, end: calendarEnd });\n    const totalPeriods = periods.length || 8;\n    const getDayInfo = (day: number) => {\n      const weekendDaysStr = systemSettings?.weekendDays || \"0:default:true,1:default:false,2:default:false,3:default:false,4:default:false,5:default:false,6:vivid:true\";\n      const parts = weekendDaysStr.split(',').filter((p: string) => p !== '');\n      const part = parts.find((p: string) => p.startsWith(`${day}:`));\n      if (part) {\n        const bits = part.split(':');\n        if (bits.length >= 3) return { themeId: bits[1], isWeekend: bits[2] === 'true' };\n        if (bits.length === 2) return { themeId: bits[1], isWeekend: true };\n      }\n      const simpleIndices = weekendDaysStr.split(',').filter((p: string) => !p.includes(':'));\n      if (simpleIndices.includes(day.toString())) return { themeId: 'default', isWeekend: true };\n      return { themeId: 'default', isWeekend: false };\n    };\n    const isWeekend = (date: Date) => getDayInfo(date.getDay()).isWeekend;\n    const holidayTheme = systemSettings?.holidayTheme || 'default';\n    const getHolidayOrWeekendTheme = (date: Date) => {\n      const holiday = getHoliday(date);\n      const dayInfo = getDayInfo(date.getDay());\n      if (dayInfo.isWeekend) return getThemeColor(colorThemes, 'HOLIDAY', dayInfo.themeId);\n      if (holiday) return getThemeColor(colorThemes, 'HOLIDAY', holidayTheme);\n      return null;\n    };\n    const getHoliday = (date: Date) => {\n      if (!date) return null;\n      const targetStr = format(date, 'yyyy-MM-dd');\n      return holidays.find((h: Holiday) => {\n        if (h.date) return h.date === targetStr;\n        if (h.start && h.end) return targetStr >= h.start && targetStr <= h.end;\n        return false;\n      });\n    };\n    let maxOverlaps = 1;\n    const dayPlacementsMap = new Map<number, any[]>();\n    days.forEach((day, dayIdx) => {\n      const dateStr = format(day, 'yyyy-MM-dd');\n      const dayLessons = lessons.filter((l: Lesson) => {\n        const subIds = [...(l.subTeacherIds || []), ...(l.subTeachers || []).map((t: any) => t.id)];\n        return (l.teacherId === userResourceId || subIds.includes(userResourceId)) && \n               dateStr >= l.startDate && dateStr <= l.endDate;\n      });\n      const dayEvents = events.filter((e: ScheduleEvent) => {\n        const resourceIdList = [...(e.resourceIds || []), ...(e.resources || []).map((r: Resource) => r.id)];\n        return resourceIdList.includes(userResourceId) && dateStr >= e.startDate && dateStr <= e.endDate;\n      });\n      const dayItems = [\n        ...dayLessons.map((l: Lesson) => {\n          let startIdx = 0, endIdx = totalPeriods - 1;\n          if (dateStr === l.startDate) {\n            const pIdx = periods.findIndex(p => p.id === l.startPeriodId);\n            startIdx = pIdx !== -1 ? pIdx : 0;\n          }\n          if (dateStr === l.endDate) {\n            const pIdx = periods.findIndex(p => p.id === l.endPeriodId);\n            endIdx = pIdx !== -1 ? pIdx : totalPeriods - 1;\n          }\n          return { type: 'lesson', data: l, startIdx, endIdx };\n        }),\n        ...dayEvents.map((e: ScheduleEvent) => {\n          let startIdx = 0, endIdx = totalPeriods - 1;\n          if (dateStr === e.startDate) {\n            const pIdx = periods.findIndex(p => p.id === e.startPeriodId);\n            startIdx = pIdx !== -1 ? pIdx : 0;\n          }\n          if (dateStr === e.endDate) {\n            const pIdx = periods.findIndex(p => p.id === e.endPeriodId);\n            endIdx = pIdx !== -1 ? pIdx : totalPeriods - 1;\n          }\n          return { type: 'event', data: e, startIdx, endIdx };\n        })\n      ];\n      if (dayItems.length > 0) {\n        const placements: any[] = [];\n        const sortedItems = [...dayItems].sort((a, b) => a.startIdx - b.startIdx || (b.endIdx - b.startIdx) - (a.endIdx - a.startIdx));\n        sortedItems.forEach(item => {\n          let level = 0;\n          while (placements.some(p => p.level === level && !(item.endIdx < p.startIdx || item.startIdx > p.endIdx))) level++;\n          placements.push({ ...item, level });\n        });\n        placements.forEach(p => {\n          const overlapping = placements.filter(other => !(p.endIdx < other.startIdx || p.startIdx > other.endIdx));\n          p.maxLevelInGroup = Math.max(...overlapping.map(o => o.level)) + 1;\n        });\n        const dayMaxLevel = placements.length > 0 ? Math.max(...placements.map(p => p.level)) + 1 : 1;\n        if (dayMaxLevel > maxOverlaps) maxOverlaps = dayMaxLevel;\n        dayPlacementsMap.set(dayIdx, placements);\n      }\n    });\n    for (let i = 1; i <= 7 * maxOverlaps; i++) {\n      worksheet.getColumn(i).width = 30 / maxOverlaps;\n    }\n    const weekdayFormatter = new Intl.DateTimeFormat(navigator.language, { weekday: 'short' });\n    const headerRow = worksheet.getRow(1);\n    headerRow.height = 30;\n    for (let i = 0; i < 7; i++) {\n      const d = new Date(2021, 0, 3 + i);\n      const startCol = i * maxOverlaps + 1;\n      const endCol = startCol + maxOverlaps - 1;\n      const cell = worksheet.getCell(1, startCol);\n      cell.value = weekdayFormatter.format(d);\n      cell.alignment = { horizontal: 'center', vertical: 'middle' };\n      cell.font = { bold: true };\n      cell.fill = { type: 'pattern', pattern: 'solid', fgColor: { argb: 'FFE0E0E0' } };\n      cell.border = { bottom: { style: 'thin' }, left: { style: 'thin' }, right: { style: 'thin' }, top: { style: 'thin' } };\n      if (endCol > startCol) worksheet.mergeCells(1, startCol, 1, endCol);\n    }\n    const weeksCount = Math.ceil(days.length / 7);\n    for (let w = 0; w < weeksCount; w++) {\n      const baseRow = 2 + w * (totalPeriods + 1);\n      for (let d = 0; d < 7; d++) {\n        const dayIdx = w * 7 + d;\n        const day = days[dayIdx];\n        if (!day) continue;\n        const colStart = (d * maxOverlaps) + 1;\n        const colEnd = colStart + maxOverlaps - 1;\n        const cell = worksheet.getCell(baseRow, colStart);\n        const isCurrMonth = isSameMonth(day, monthStart);\n        const holiday = getHoliday(day);\n        const hTheme = getHolidayOrWeekendTheme(day);\n        cell.value = `${format(day, 'd')}${holiday ? ` (${roomLabel})` : ''}`;\n            const hasTeacher = !!(l.teacherId || l.externalTeacher);\n            const theme = getThemeColor(colorThemes, 'LESSON', hasTeacher ? (resources.find(r => r.id === l.roomId)?.name || '') : (l.location || '');\n            row.getCell(6).value = l.teacherId ? else break;\n            }\n            row.getCell(3).value = t(l.subject);\n            row.getCell(4).value = (l.deliveryMethods || []).map(m => m.name).join(', ');\n            row.getCell(5).value = l.roomId ? (resources.find(r => r.id === l.roomId)?.name || '') : (l.location || '');\n            row.getCell(6).value = l.teacherId ? i <= 7; i++) {\n          const cell = row.getCell(i);\n          cell.alignment = { vertical: 'middle', horizontal: i <= 2 ? i <= 6; i++) xlRow.getCell(i).fill = { type: 'pattern', pattern: 'solid', fgColor: { argb: row.level === 1 ? 'FFF5F5F5' : 'FFF9F9F9' } };\n        }\n        if (row.level === 1) { totalAssigned += row.assigned; totalScheduled += row.scheduled; }\n        for (let i = 1; i <= 6; i++) {\n          const cell = xlRow.getCell(i);\n          cell.border = { top: { style: 'thin' }, left: { style: 'thin' }, bottom: { style: 'thin' }, right: { style: 'thin' } };\n          if (i >= 4) cell.alignment = { horizontal: 'right' };\n        }\n        currentRowIdx++;\n        if (row.children) addRows(row.children);\n      });\n    };\n    addRows(stats);\n    const footerRow = worksheet.getRow(currentRowIdx);\n    footerRow.getCell(1).value = t('Grand Total');\n    worksheet.mergeCells(currentRowIdx, 1, currentRowIdx, 3);\n    footerRow.getCell(4).value = totalAssigned;\n    footerRow.getCell(5).value = totalScheduled;\n    footerRow.getCell(6).value = totalScheduled - totalAssigned;\n    footerRow.font = { bold: true };\n    for (let i = 1; i <= 6; i++) {\n      const cell = footerRow.getCell(i);\n      cell.fill = { type: 'pattern', pattern: 'solid', fgColor: { argb: 'FFE0E0E0' } };\n      cell.border = { top: { style: 'medium' }, left: { style: 'thin' }, bottom: { style: 'medium' }, right: { style: 'thin' } };\n      if (i >= 4) cell.alignment = { horizontal: 'right' };\n    }\n    const buffer = await workbook.xlsx.writeBuffer();\n    saveAs(new Blob([buffer]), \\`Statistics_\\${courseName}_\\${format(new Date(), 'yyyyMMdd')}.xlsx\\`);\n  } catch (err) { console.error('Course Statistics Export Error:', err); }\n}\nEOF\nrm src/utils/excelExport.ts && mv tmp_excel.ts src/utils/excelExport.ts"
  }
}

i <= 7; i++) {\n          const cell = row.getCell(i);\n          cell.alignment = { vertical: 'middle', horizontal: i <= 2 ? 'center' : 'left', wrapText: true };\n          cell.border = { top: { style: 'thin' }, left: { style: 'thin' }, bottom: { style: 'thin' }, right: { style: 'thin' } };\n        }\n        currentRowIdx++;\n      });\n      if (periods.length > 1) worksheet.mergeCells(startRowForDay, 1, currentRowIdx - 1, 1);\n    });\n    const buffer = await workbook.xlsx.writeBuffer();\n    saveAs(new Blob([buffer]), `WeeklySchedule_${t(course.name)}_${format(weekStart, 'yyyyMMdd')}.xlsx`);\n  } catch (err) { console.error('Course Weekly Export Error:', err); }\n}\n\nexport async function exportCourseStatisticsToExcel({\n  courseName, stats, labels, t\n}: {\n  courseName: string;\n  stats: any[];\n  labels: ResourceLabels;\n  t: (key: string, options?: any) => string;\n}) {\n  try {\n    const workbook = new ExcelJS.Workbook();\n    const worksheet = workbook.addWorksheet('Statistics');\n    worksheet.mergeCells(1, 1, 1, 6);\n    const titleCell = worksheet.getCell(1, 1);\n    titleCell.value = `${t('Course Statistics')}: ${courseName}`;\n    titleCell.font = { bold: true, size: 14 };\n    titleCell.alignment = { horizontal: 'center' };\n    const headers = [labels.subjectLarge, labels.subjectMiddle, labels.subjectSmall, t('Assigned'), t('Scheduled'), t('Diff')];\n    const headerRow = worksheet.getRow(3);\n    headers.forEach((h, i) => {\n      const cell = headerRow.getCell(i + 1);\n      cell.value = h;\n      cell.font = { bold: true };\n      cell.fill = { type: 'pattern', pattern: 'solid', fgColor: { argb: 'FFE0E0E0' } };\n      cell.border = { top: { style: 'thin' }, left: { style: 'thin' }, bottom: { style: 'thin' }, right: { style: 'thin' } };\n      cell.alignment = { horizontal: 'center' };\n    });\n    worksheet.getColumn(1).width = 25; worksheet.getColumn(2).width = 25; worksheet.getColumn(3).width = 30;\n    worksheet.getColumn(4).width = 12; worksheet.getColumn(5).width = 12; worksheet.getColumn(6).width = 12;\n    let currentRowIdx = 4;\n    let totalAssigned = 0;\n    let totalScheduled = 0;\n    const addRows = (rows: any[]) => {\n      rows.forEach(row => {\n        const xlRow = worksheet.getRow(currentRowIdx);\n        xlRow.getCell(1).value = row.level === 1 ? row.name : '';\n        xlRow.getCell(2).value = row.level === 2 ? row.name : '';\n        xlRow.getCell(3).value = row.level === 3 ? row.name : '';\n        xlRow.getCell(4).value = row.assigned;\n        xlRow.getCell(5).value = row.scheduled;\n        xlRow.getCell(6).value = row.scheduled - row.assigned;\n        const isGroup = row.children && row.children.length > 0;\n        if (isGroup || row.level === 1) {\n          xlRow.font = { bold: true };\n          for (let i = 1; i <= 6; i++) xlRow.getCell(i).fill = { type: 'pattern', pattern: 'solid', fgColor: { argb: row.level === 1 ? 'FFF5F5F5' : 'FFF9F9F9' } };\n        }\n        if (row.level === 1) { totalAssigned += row.assigned; totalScheduled += row.scheduled; }\n        for (let i = 1; i <= 6; i++) {\n          const cell = xlRow.getCell(i);\n          cell.border = { top: { style: 'thin' }, left: { style: 'thin' }, bottom: { style: 'thin' }, right: { style: 'thin' } };\n          if (i >= 4) cell.alignment = { horizontal: 'right' };\n        }\n        currentRowIdx++;\n        if (row.children) addRows(row.children);\n      });\n    };\n    addRows(stats);\n    const footerRow = worksheet.getRow(currentRowIdx);\n    footerRow.getCell(1).value = t('Grand Total');\n    worksheet.mergeCells(currentRowIdx, 1, currentRowIdx, 3);\n    footerRow.getCell(4).value = totalAssigned;\n    footerRow.getCell(5).value = totalScheduled;\n    footerRow.getCell(6).value = totalScheduled - totalAssigned;\n    footerRow.font = { bold: true };\n    for (let i = 1; i <= 6; i++) {\n      const cell = footerRow.getCell(i);\n      cell.fill = { type: 'pattern', pattern: 'solid', fgColor: { argb: 'FFE0E0E0' } };\n      cell.border = { top: { style: 'medium' }, left: { style: 'thin' }, bottom: { style: 'medium' }, right: { style: 'thin' } };\n      if (i >= 4) cell.alignment = { horizontal: 'right' };\n    }\n    const buffer = await workbook.xlsx.writeBuffer();\n    saveAs(new Blob([buffer]), `Statistics_${courseName}_${format(new Date(), 'yyyyMMdd')}.xlsx`);\n  } catch (err) { console.error('Course Statistics Export Error:', err); }\n}\n\ninterface PersonalExportParams {\n  userResourceId: string;\n  periods: TimePeriod[];\n  resources: Resource[];\n  lessons: Lesson[];\n  events: ScheduleEvent[];\n  baseDate: Date;\n  holidays: Holiday[];\n  labels: ResourceLabels;\n  systemSettings: SystemSetting | null;\n  colorThemes: ColorTheme[];\n  t: (key: string, options?: any) => string;\n}\n\nexport async function exportPersonalMonthlyToExcel({\n  userResourceId, periods, resources, lessons, events, baseDate, holidays, labels, systemSettings, colorThemes, t\n}: PersonalExportParams) {\n  try {\n    const workbook = new ExcelJS.Workbook();\n    const worksheet = workbook.addWorksheet('My Schedule');\n\n    const monthStart = startOfMonth(baseDate);\n    const monthEnd = endOfMonth(monthStart);\n    const calendarStart = startOfWeek(monthStart, { weekStartsOn: 0 });\n    const calendarEnd = endOfWeek(monthEnd, { weekStartsOn: 0 });\n    const days = eachDayOfInterval({ start: calendarStart, end: calendarEnd });\n\n    const totalPeriods = periods.length || 8;\n    \n    const getDayInfo = (day: number) => {\n      const weekendDaysStr = systemSettings?.weekendDays || \"0:default:true,1:default:false,2:default:false,3:default:false,4:default:false,5:default:false,6:vivid:true\";\n      const parts = weekendDaysStr.split(',').filter((p: string) => p !== '');\n      const part = parts.find((p: string) => p.startsWith(`${day}:`));\n      if (part) {\n        const bits = part.split(':');\n        if (bits.length >= 3) return { themeId: bits[1], isWeekend: bits[2] === 'true' };\n        if (bits.length === 2) return { themeId: bits[1], isWeekend: true };\n      }\n      const simpleIndices = weekendDaysStr.split(',').filter((p: string) => !p.includes(':'));\n      if (simpleIndices.includes(day.toString())) return { themeId: 'default', isWeekend: true };\n      return { themeId: 'default', isWeekend: false };\n    };\n\n    const isWeekend = (date: Date) => getDayInfo(date.getDay()).isWeekend;\n    const holidayTheme = systemSettings?.holidayTheme || 'default';\n\n    const getHolidayOrWeekendTheme = (date: Date) => {\n      const holiday = getHoliday(date);\n      const dayInfo = getDayInfo(date.getDay());\n      if (dayInfo.isWeekend) return getThemeColor(colorThemes, 'HOLIDAY', dayInfo.themeId);\n      if (holiday) return getThemeColor(colorThemes, 'HOLIDAY', holidayTheme);\n      return null;\n    };\n\n    const getHoliday = (date: Date) => {\n      if (!date) return null;\n      const targetStr = format(date, 'yyyy-MM-dd');\n      return holidays.find((h: Holiday) => {\n        if (h.date) return h.date === targetStr;\n        if (h.start && h.end) return targetStr >= h.start && targetStr <= h.end;\n        return false;\n      });\n    };\n    \n    let maxOverlaps = 1;\n    const dayPlacementsMap = new Map<number, any[]>();\n\n    days.forEach((day, dayIdx) => {\n      const dateStr = format(day, 'yyyy-MM-dd');\n      const dayLessons = lessons.filter((l: Lesson) => {\n        const subIds = [...(l.subTeacherIds || []), ...(l.subTeachers || []).map((t: any) => t.id)];\n        return (l.teacherId === userResourceId || subIds.includes(userResourceId)) && \n               dateStr >= l.startDate && dateStr <= l.endDate;\n      });\n      const dayEvents = events.filter((e: ScheduleEvent) => {\n        const resourceIdList = [...(e.resourceIds || []), ...(e.resources || []).map((r: Resource) => r.id)];\n        return resourceIdList.includes(userResourceId) && dateStr >= e.startDate && dateStr <= e.endDate;\n      });\n\n      const dayItems = [\n        ...dayLessons.map((l: Lesson) => {\n          let startIdx = 0, endIdx = totalPeriods - 1;\n          if (dateStr === l.startDate) {\n            const pIdx = periods.findIndex(p => p.id === l.startPeriodId);\n            startIdx = pIdx !== -1 ? pIdx : 0;\n          }\n          if (dateStr === l.endDate) {\n            const pIdx = periods.findIndex(p => p.id === l.endPeriodId);\n            endIdx = pIdx !== -1 ? pIdx : totalPeriods - 1;\n          }\n          return { type: 'lesson', data: l, startIdx, endIdx };\n        }),\n        ...dayEvents.map((e: ScheduleEvent) => {\n          let startIdx = 0, endIdx = totalPeriods - 1;\n          if (dateStr === e.startDate) {\n            const pIdx = periods.findIndex(p => p.id === e.startPeriodId);\n            startIdx = pIdx !== -1 ? pIdx : 0;\n          }\n          if (dateStr === e.endDate) {\n            const pIdx = periods.findIndex(p => p.id === e.endPeriodId);\n            endIdx = pIdx !== -1 ? pIdx : totalPeriods - 1;\n          }\n          return { type: 'event', data: e, startIdx, endIdx };\n        })\n      ];\n\n      if (dayItems.length > 0) {\n        const placements: any[] = [];\n        const sortedItems = [...dayItems].sort((a, b) => a.startIdx - b.startIdx || (b.endIdx - b.startIdx) - (a.endIdx - a.startIdx));\n        sortedItems.forEach(item => {\n          let level = 0;\n          while (placements.some(p => p.level === level && !(item.endIdx < p.startIdx || item.startIdx > p.endIdx))) level++;\n          placements.push({ ...item, level });\n        });\n        placements.forEach(p => {\n          const overlapping = placements.filter(other => !(p.endIdx < other.startIdx || p.startIdx > other.endIdx));\n          p.maxLevelInGroup = Math.max(...overlapping.map(o => o.level)) + 1;\n        });\n        const dayMaxLevel = placements.length > 0 ? Math.max(...placements.map(p => p.level)) + 1 : 1;\n        if (dayMaxLevel > maxOverlaps) maxOverlaps = dayMaxLevel;\n        dayPlacementsMap.set(dayIdx, placements);\n      }\n    });\n    for (let i = 1; i <= 7 * maxOverlaps; i++) {\n      worksheet.getColumn(i).width = 30 / maxOverlaps;\n    }\n    const weekdayFormatter = new Intl.DateTimeFormat(navigator.language, { weekday: 'short' });\n    const headerRow = worksheet.getRow(1);\n    headerRow.height = 30;\n    for (let i = 0; i < 7; i++) {\n      const d = new Date(2021, 0, 3 + i);\n      const startCol = i * maxOverlaps + 1;\n      const endCol = startCol + maxOverlaps - 1;\n      const cell = worksheet.getCell(1, startCol);\n      cell.value = weekdayFormatter.format(d);\n      cell.alignment = { horizontal: 'center', vertical: 'middle' };\n      cell.font = { bold: true };\n      cell.fill = { type: 'pattern', pattern: 'solid', fgColor: { argb: 'FFE0E0E0' } };\n      cell.border = { bottom: { style: 'thin' }, left: { style: 'thin' }, right: { style: 'thin' }, top: { style: 'thin' } };\n      if (endCol > startCol) worksheet.mergeCells(1, startCol, 1, endCol);\n    }\n    const weeksCount = Math.ceil(days.length / 7);\n    for (let w = 0; w < weeksCount; w++) {\n      const baseRow = 2 + w * (totalPeriods + 1);\n      for (let d = 0; d < 7; d++) {\n        const dayIdx = w * 7 + d;\n        const day = days[dayIdx];\n        if (!day) continue;\n        const colStart = (d * maxOverlaps) + 1;\n        const colEnd = colStart + maxOverlaps - 1;\n        const cell = worksheet.getCell(baseRow, colStart);\n        const isCurrMonth = isSameMonth(day, monthStart);\n        const holiday = getHoliday(day);\n        const hTheme = getHolidayOrWeekendTheme(day);\n        cell.value = `${format(day, 'd')}${holiday ? ` (${holiday.name})` : ''}`;\n        cell.font = { bold: true, size: 10 };\n        cell.alignment = { horizontal: 'left', vertical: 'middle' };\n        let bgColor = 'FFFFFFFF', textColor = 'FF000000';\n        if (hTheme) { bgColor = hexToARGB(hTheme.background); textColor = hexToARGB(hTheme.foreground); } \n        else if (!isCurrMonth) bgColor = 'FFF0F0F0';\n        cell.fill = { type: 'pattern', pattern: 'solid', fgColor: { argb: bgColor } };\n        cell.font = { ...cell.font, color: { argb: textColor } };\n        cell.border = { left: { style: 'thin' }, right: { style: 'thin' }, top: { style: 'thin' }, bottom: { style: 'thin' } };\n        if (colEnd > colStart) worksheet.mergeCells(baseRow, colStart, baseRow, colEnd);\n        for (let p = 1; p <= totalPeriods; p++) {\n          for (let sc = 0; sc < maxOverlaps; sc++) {\n            const pCell = worksheet.getCell(baseRow + p, colStart + sc);\n            pCell.fill = { type: 'pattern', pattern: 'solid', fgColor: { argb: bgColor } };\n            pCell.border = { left: sc === 0 ? { style: 'thin' } : undefined, right: sc === maxOverlaps - 1 ? { style: 'thin' } : undefined, bottom: p === totalPeriods ? { style: 'thin' } : undefined };\n          }\n          worksheet.getRow(baseRow + p).height = 30;\n        }\n        const placements = dayPlacementsMap.get(dayIdx) || [];\n        placements.forEach(placement => {\n          const { type, data, startIdx, endIdx, level, maxLevelInGroup } = placement;\n          const colsPerLevel = maxOverlaps / maxLevelInGroup;\n          const itemColStart = colStart + Math.floor(level * colsPerLevel);\n          const itemColEnd = colStart + Math.floor((level + 1) * colsPerLevel) - 1;\n          const startRow = baseRow + 1 + startIdx, span = endIdx - startIdx + 1, endRow = startRow + span - 1;\n          const cell = worksheet.getCell(startRow, itemColStart);\n          const periodLabel = span > 1 ? `${startIdx + 1}-${endIdx + 1}` : `${startIdx + 1}`;\n          if (type === 'event') {\n            const e = data as ScheduleEvent;\n            cell.value = `[${periodLabel}] ${e.name}${e.location ? ` (${e.location})` : ''}`;\n            const theme = getThemeColor(colorThemes, 'EVENT', e.name);\n            const bgColor = e.color || theme?.background || '#fef3c7', textColor = theme?.foreground || '#000000';\n            cell.fill = { type: 'pattern', pattern: 'solid', fgColor: { argb: hexToARGB(bgColor) } };\n            cell.font = { color: { argb: hexToARGB(textColor) } };\n          } else {\n            const l = data as Lesson;\n            const room = resources.find(r => r.id === l.roomId), roomLabel = room?.name || l.location || '';\n            cell.value = `[${periodLabel}] ${l.subject}${roomLabel ? ` (${roomLabel})` : ''}`;\n            const hasTeacher = !!(l.teacherId || l.externalTeacher);\n            const theme = getThemeColor(colorThemes, 'LESSON', hasTeacher ? 'with-teacher' : 'no-teacher');\n            const bgColor = theme?.background || (hasTeacher ? '#646cff' : '#e884fa'), textColor = theme?.foreground || '#ffffff';\n            cell.fill = { type: 'pattern', pattern: 'solid', fgColor: { argb: hexToARGB(bgColor) } };\n            cell.font = { color: { argb: hexToARGB(textColor) } };\n          }\n          cell.alignment = { horizontal: 'center', vertical: 'middle', wrapText: true };\n          cell.border = { bottom: { style: 'thin' }, left: { style: 'thin' }, right: { style: 'thin' }, top: { style: 'thin' } };\n          try { worksheet.mergeCells(startRow, itemColStart, endRow, itemColEnd); } catch (e) { console.warn('Merge failed in Personal Export:', e); }\n        });\n      }\n    }\n    const buffer = await workbook.xlsx.writeBuffer();\n    saveAs(new Blob([buffer]), `PersonalSchedule_${format(baseDate, 'yyyyMM')}.xlsx`);\n  } catch (err) { console.error('Personal Export Error:', err); }\n}\n\nexport async function exportCourseWeeklyToExcel({\n  courseId, periods, resources, lessons, baseDate, labels, t\n}: {\n  courseId: string;\n  periods: TimePeriod[];\n  resources: Resource[];\n  lessons: Lesson[];\n  baseDate: Date;\n  labels: ResourceLabels;\n  t: (key: string, options?: any) => string;\n}) {\n  try {\n    const workbook = new ExcelJS.Workbook();\n    const worksheet = workbook.addWorksheet('Weekly Schedule');\n    const course = resources.find(r => r.id === courseId);\n    if (!course) return;\n    worksheet.mergeCells(1, 1, 1, 7);\n    const titleCell = worksheet.getCell(1, 1);\n    titleCell.value = t(course.name);\n    titleCell.font = { bold: true, size: 14 };\n    titleCell.alignment = { horizontal: 'center' };\n    const headers = [t('Date'), t('Period'), labels.subject, labels.deliveryMethod, labels.room, labels.mainTeacher, t('Remarks')];\n    const headerRow = worksheet.getRow(4);\n    headers.forEach((h, i) => {\n      const cell = headerRow.getCell(i + 1);\n      cell.value = h;\n      cell.font = { bold: true };\n      cell.fill = { type: 'pattern', pattern: 'solid', fgColor: { argb: 'FFE0E0E0' } };\n      cell.border = { top: { style: 'thin' }, left: { style: 'thin' }, bottom: { style: 'thin' }, right: { style: 'thin' } };\n    });\n    worksheet.getColumn(1).width = 15; worksheet.getColumn(2).width = 10; worksheet.getColumn(3).width = 50; \n    worksheet.getColumn(4).width = 20; worksheet.getColumn(5).width = 20; worksheet.getColumn(6).width = 20; worksheet.getColumn(7).width = 15;\n    const weekStart = startOfWeek(baseDate, { weekStartsOn: 0 });\n    const weekEnd = addDays(weekStart, 6);\n    const displayDates = eachDayOfInterval({ start: weekStart, end: weekEnd });\n    let currentRowIdx = 5;\n    displayDates.forEach(date => {\n      const dateStr = format(date, 'yyyy-MM-dd');\n      const dayLessons = lessons.filter(l => l.courseId === courseId && dateStr >= l.startDate && dateStr <= l.endDate);\n      const startRowForDay = currentRowIdx;\n      const processedLessonIds = new Set<string>();\n      const processedEmptyStartIndices = new Set<number>();\n      periods.forEach((period, pIdx) => {\n        const row = worksheet.getRow(currentRowIdx);\n        row.getCell(1).value = format(date, t('date_format'), { locale: t('locale') === 'ja' ? ja : undefined });\n        row.getCell(2).value = period.name.replace(/\\D/g, '');\n        const l = dayLessons.find(dl => {\n          if (dateStr === dl.startDate && dateStr === dl.endDate) return period.id >= dl.startPeriodId && period.id <= dl.endPeriodId;\n          if (dateStr === dl.startDate) return period.id >= dl.startPeriodId;\n          if (dateStr === dl.endDate) return period.id <= dl.endPeriodId;\n          return dateStr > dl.startDate && dateStr < dl.endDate;\n        });\n        if (l) {\n          if (!processedLessonIds.has(l.id)) {\n            processedLessonIds.add(l.id);\n            let span = 1;\n            for (let nextPIdx = pIdx + 1; nextPIdx < periods.length; nextPIdx++) {\n              const nextPeriod = periods[nextPIdx];\n              const isSame = dayLessons.some(dl => dl.id === l.id && (() => {\n                if (dateStr === dl.startDate && dateStr === dl.endDate) return nextPeriod.id >= dl.startPeriodId && nextPeriod.id <= dl.endPeriodId;\n                if (dateStr === dl.startDate) return nextPeriod.id >= dl.startPeriodId;\n                if (dateStr === dl.endDate) return nextPeriod.id <= dl.endPeriodId;\n                return dateStr > dl.startDate && dateStr < dl.endDate;\n              })());\n              if (isSame) span++; else break;\n            }\n            row.getCell(3).value = t(l.subject);\n            row.getCell(4).value = (l.deliveryMethods || []).map(m => m.name).join(', ');\n            row.getCell(5).value = l.roomId ? (resources.find(r => r.id === l.roomId)?.name || '') : (l.location || '');\n            row.getCell(6).value = l.teacherId ? (resources.find(r => r.id === l.teacherId)?.name || '') : (l.externalTeacher || '');\n            row.getCell(7).value = l.remarks || '';\n            if (span > 1) for (let col = 3; col <= 7; col++) worksheet.mergeCells(currentRowIdx, col, currentRowIdx + span - 1, col);\n          }\n        } else {\n          const isAlreadyProcessed = Array.from(processedEmptyStartIndices).some(startIdx => {\n            let emptySpan = 0;\n            for (let i = startIdx; i < periods.length; i++) {\n              const hasLesson = dayLessons.some(dl => {\n                const p = periods[i];\n                if (dateStr === dl.startDate && dateStr === dl.endDate) return p.id >= dl.startPeriodId && p.id <= dl.endPeriodId;\n                if (dateStr === dl.startDate) return p.id >= dl.startPeriodId;\n                if (dateStr === dl.endDate) return p.id <= dl.endPeriodId;\n                return dateStr > dl.startDate && dateStr < dl.endDate;\n              });\n              if (!hasLesson) emptySpan++; else break;\n            }\n            return pIdx >= startIdx && pIdx < startIdx + emptySpan;\n          });\n          if (!isAlreadyProcessed) {\n            let emptySpan = 1;\n            for (let nextPIdx = pIdx + 1; nextPIdx < periods.length; nextPIdx++) {\n              const nextPeriod = periods[nextPIdx];\n              const nextLesson = dayLessons.find(dl => {\n                if (dateStr === dl.startDate && dateStr === dl.endDate) return nextPeriod.id >= dl.startPeriodId && nextPeriod.id <= dl.endPeriodId;\n                if (dateStr === dl.startDate) return nextPeriod.id >= dl.startPeriodId;\n                if (dateStr === dl.endDate) return nextPeriod.id <= dl.endPeriodId;\n                return dateStr > dl.startDate && dateStr < dl.endDate;\n              });\n              if (!nextLesson) emptySpan++; else break;\n            }\n            for (let i = 3; i <= 7; i++) row.getCell(i).value = '';\n            if (emptySpan > 1) for (let col = 3; col <= 7; col++) worksheet.mergeCells(currentRowIdx, col, currentRowIdx + emptySpan - 1, col);\n            processedEmptyStartIndices.add(pIdx);\n          }\n        }\n        for (let i = 1; i <= 7; i++) {\n          const cell = row.getCell(i);\n          cell.alignment = { vertical: 'middle', horizontal: i <= 2 ? 'center' : 'left', wrapText: true };\n          cell.border = { top: { style: 'thin' }, left: { style: 'thin' }, bottom: { style: 'thin' }, right: { style: 'thin' } };\n        }\n        currentRowIdx++;\n      });\n      if (periods.length > 1) worksheet.mergeCells(startRowForDay, 1, currentRowIdx - 1, 1);\n    });\n    const buffer = await workbook.xlsx.writeBuffer();\n    saveAs(new Blob([buffer]), `WeeklySchedule_${t(course.name)}_${format(weekStart, 'yyyyMMdd')}.xlsx`);\n  } catch (err) { console.error('Course Weekly Export Error:', err); }\n}\n\nexport async function exportCourseStatisticsToExcel({\n  courseName, stats, labels, t\n}: {\n  courseName: string;\n  stats: any[];\n  labels: ResourceLabels;\n  t: (key: string, options?: any) => string;\n}) {\n  try {\n    const workbook = new ExcelJS.Workbook();\n    const worksheet = workbook.addWorksheet('Statistics');\n    worksheet.mergeCells(1, 1, 1, 6);\n    const titleCell = worksheet.getCell(1, 1);\n    titleCell.value = `${t('Course Statistics')}: ${courseName}`;\n    titleCell.font = { bold: true, size: 14 };\n    titleCell.alignment = { horizontal: 'center' };\n    const headers = [labels.subjectLarge, labels.subjectMiddle, labels.subjectSmall, t('Assigned'), t('Scheduled'), t('Diff')];\n    const headerRow = worksheet.getRow(3);\n    headers.forEach((h, i) => {\n      const cell = headerRow.getCell(i + 1);\n      cell.value = h;\n      cell.font = { bold: true };\n      cell.fill = { type: 'pattern', pattern: 'solid', fgColor: { argb: 'FFE0E0E0' } };\n      cell.border = { top: { style: 'thin' }, left: { style: 'thin' }, bottom: { style: 'thin' }, right: { style: 'thin' } };\n      cell.alignment = { horizontal: 'center' };\n    });\n    worksheet.getColumn(1).width = 25; worksheet.getColumn(2).width = 25; worksheet.getColumn(3).width = 30;\n    worksheet.getColumn(4).width = 12; worksheet.getColumn(5).width = 12; worksheet.getColumn(6).width = 12;\n    let currentRowIdx = 4;\n    let totalAssigned = 0;\n    let totalScheduled = 0;\n    const addRows = (rows: any[]) => {\n      rows.forEach(row => {\n        const xlRow = worksheet.getRow(currentRowIdx);\n        xlRow.getCell(1).value = row.level === 1 ? row.name : '';\n        xlRow.getCell(2).value = row.level === 2 ? row.name : '';\n        xlRow.getCell(3).value = row.level === 3 ? row.name : '';\n        xlRow.getCell(4).value = row.assigned;\n        xlRow.getCell(5).value = row.scheduled;\n        xlRow.getCell(6).value = row.scheduled - row.assigned;\n        const isGroup = row.children && row.children.length > 0;\n        if (isGroup || row.level === 1) {\n          xlRow.font = { bold: true };\n          for (let i = 1; i <= 6; i++) xlRow.getCell(i).fill = { type: 'pattern', pattern: 'solid', fgColor: { argb: row.level === 1 ? 'FFF5F5F5' : 'FFF9F9F9' } };\n        }\n        if (row.level === 1) { totalAssigned += row.assigned; totalScheduled += row.scheduled; }\n        for (let i = 1; i <= 6; i++) {\n          const cell = xlRow.getCell(i);\n          cell.border = { top: { style: 'thin' }, left: { style: 'thin' }, bottom: { style: 'thin' }, right: { style: 'thin' } };\n          if (i >= 4) cell.alignment = { horizontal: 'right' };\n        }\n        currentRowIdx++;\n        if (row.children) addRows(row.children);\n      });\n    };\n    addRows(stats);\n    const footerRow = worksheet.getRow(currentRowIdx);\n    footerRow.getCell(1).value = t('Grand Total');\n    worksheet.mergeCells(currentRowIdx, 1, currentRowIdx, 3);\n    footerRow.getCell(4).value = totalAssigned;\n    footerRow.getCell(5).value = totalScheduled;\n    footerRow.getCell(6).value = totalScheduled - totalAssigned;\n    footerRow.font = { bold: true };\n    for (let i = 1; i <= 6; i++) {\n      const cell = footerRow.getCell(i);\n      cell.fill = { type: 'pattern', pattern: 'solid', fgColor: { argb: 'FFE0E0E0' } };\n      cell.border = { top: { style: 'medium' }, left: { style: 'thin' }, bottom: { style: 'medium' }, right: { style: 'thin' } };\n      if (i >= 4) cell.alignment = { horizontal: 'right' };\n    }\n    const buffer = await workbook.xlsx.writeBuffer();\n    saveAs(new Blob([buffer]), `Statistics_${courseName}_${format(new Date(), 'yyyyMMdd')}.xlsx`);\n  } catch (err) { console.error('Course Statistics Export Error:', err); }\n}\nProcess Group PGID: 178479"
  }
}
```

## MODEL ✨

**Tool Command**:

   const dayInfo = getDayInfo(date.getDay());\n    if (dayInfo.isWeekend) return getThemeColor(colorThemes, 'HOLIDAY', dayInfo.themeId);\n    if (holiday) return getThemeColor(colorThemes, 'HOLIDAY', holidayTheme);\n    return null;\n  };\n\n  const getHoliday = (date: Date) => {\n    if (!date) return null;\n    const targetStr = format(date, 'yyyy-MM-dd');\n    return holidays.find((h: Holiday)
